## Patch notes

These are the official patch notes for [Path of Exile 2](/wiki/Path_of_Exile_2 "Path of Exile 2") **version 0.4.0** released by [Grinding Gear Games](/wiki/Grinding_Gear_Games "Grinding Gear Games").[[1]](#cite_note-Patch_Notes-1)

> ### The Fate of the Vaal League
>
> Start fresh in a new economy with [The Fate of the Vaal league](/wiki/Fate_of_the_Vaal_league "Fate of the Vaal league"). All of your old characters from [Early Access](/wiki/Early_Access "Early Access") are still present in the Early Access leagues but a free passive tree refund has been granted due to the changes. We would highly encourage you to join the new leagues to fully take in the changes we've made with the 0.4.0 update.
>
> * In the Fate of the Vaal league you will find remnants of the ancient [Vaal](/wiki/Vaal/edit?redlink=1 "Vaal (page does not exist)") civilisation scattered throughout [Wraeclast](/wiki/Wraeclast "Wraeclast").
> * Now that corruption has returned to the land, the long-dead Vaal structures throughout Wraeclast are activating and affecting nearby creatures. Sacrifice the afflicted monsters to power the devices, and travel to [Lira Vaal](/wiki/Atziri%27s_Temple "Atziri's Temple"), the ancient temple of [Atziri](/wiki/Atziri "Atziri"). Gather enough power to modify the Temple and create your desired layout. Each room in the Temple offers great rewards, from stashes of currency and equipment to something more interesting. Placing rooms next to other rooms that benefit them will level them up, adding new challenges and rewards to find. Complete more beacons to get more energy to fuel more additions to the temple. Explore the Queen of the Vaal's opulent temple during the height of her power in the capital of the ancient empire. With the power of the Beast, Atziri plans to risk her entire civilization in pursuit of eternal youth. Can she be stopped? Her Royal Architect and devoted followers will work against you, but perhaps the past is not set in stone…
> * There are [Standard](/wiki/Standard "Standard"), [Hardcore](/wiki/Hardcore "Hardcore") and [Solo Self-Found](/wiki/Solo_Self-Found "Solo Self-Found") variations of The Fate of the Vaal League available. They have the same core [mechanics](/wiki/Mechanics/edit?redlink=1 "Mechanics (page does not exist)") and items, and you can create private league versions of these leagues.
>
> ### New Content and Features
>
> * Added a new playable [character class](/wiki/Character_class "Character class"), the [Druid](/wiki/Druid "Druid").
> * Added the new [Oracle](/wiki/Oracle "Oracle") and [Shaman](/wiki/Shaman "Shaman") [Ascendancy Classes](/wiki/Ascendancy_classes "Ascendancy classes") for the Druid.
> * Added over 20 new [Skills](/wiki/Skills "Skills"), primarily Primal Skills.
> * Added over 35 new [Supports](/wiki/Support_gem "Support gem").
> * Also introduced over 8 new [Lineage Supports](/wiki/Lineage_support_gem "Lineage support gem"), much more powerful Supports that are only available in [Endgame](/wiki/Endgame "Endgame").
> * Added over 250 new passive skills to the [passive tree](/wiki/Passive_tree "Passive tree").
> * Added over 10 new Unique Items.
> * Added a new weapon class: [Talismans](/wiki/Talisman "Talisman"). Talismans are two-handed martial weapons that are used for shapeshifting attacks. Equipping a talisman shapeshifts you into an animal form and grants you a basic attack skill for that form. You can swap your chosen form at any time.
> * Added 4 new Augment items with new [modifiers](/wiki/Modifier "Modifier") that you can craft onto your items.
> * Continued to incrementally improve the sound, art, effects and environments.
>
> ### Abyss as a Core Mechanic
>
> * [Abyss](/wiki/Abyss "Abyss") has been added to the core game. You can find Abyss encounters in specific campaign areas, starting in [Act 2](/wiki/Act_2 "Act 2"). Abyss encounters have been added to the Endgame, as well as [Abyss Tablets](/wiki/Abyss_Tablet "Abyss Tablet") and related modifiers.
> * Added an [Atlas Passive Tree](/wiki/Atlas_Passive_Tree "Atlas Passive Tree") for the [Rise of the Abyssal](/wiki/Rise_of_the_Abyssal "Rise of the Abyssal") Content.
> * ![](/images/thumb/e/e2/Preserved_Vertebrae_inventory_icon.png/16px-Preserved_Vertebrae_inventory_icon.png)[Preserved Vertebrae](/wiki/Preserved_Vertebrae "Preserved Vertebrae")Preserved VertebraeStack Size: *20*[Desecrates](/wiki/Desecrate "Desecrate") a [Rare](/wiki/Rare "Rare") [Waystone](/wiki/Waystone "Waystone")Right click this item then left click a Rare item to apply it.![](/images/thumb/e/e2/Preserved_Vertebrae_inventory_icon.png/78px-Preserved_Vertebrae_inventory_icon.png) no longer drop.
> * Updated [The Well of Souls quest](/wiki/The_Well_of_Souls_%28quest%29 "The Well of Souls (quest)") to account for the fact that Abysses no longer spawn in all campaign areas.
>
> ### General Improvements
>
> Significant optimizations to CPU performance have been made. These changes both improve the speed of key operations, and allow us to utilise more of your CPU cores, resulting in higher frame rates. Overall, you should get at least a 25% boost, and significantly less frame spikes when CPU bound. This is especially impactful for heavy gameplay situations. Note that if you are GPU bound, you will not see any improvement from these changes. When GPU bound, lowering render resolution or using Dynamic Resolution will improve performance.
>
> ### Player Changes
>
> * [Tailwind](/wiki/Tailwind "Tailwind") now grants 1% increased movement speed, 2% increased Skill Speed (previously 3%), 10% increased Evasion Rating (previously 15%) and prevent 1% of Damage from Deflected Hits per stack.
> * Base [unarmed](/wiki/Unarmed "Unarmed") attack time is now 1.65 attacks per second (previously 1.4).
> * Modifiers to the number of enemies required to be considered [Surrounded](/wiki/Surrounded "Surrounded") can no longer reduce the required number of enemies below 1.
> * [Rage](/wiki/Rage "Rage") regeneration now pauses rage decay similarly to other means of gaining rage. This means that your rage will never decay while it is regenerating.
> * All rage spending costs have been changed to 10 rage. Rage no longer causes a visual effect on your character until you have 10 or more Rage so that you know that you can use these abilities.
> * You now lose 5 [rage](/wiki/Rage "Rage") per second if you have not taken damage or gained rage in the past 4 seconds (from 10 rage per second if not taken damage or gained rage in the past 2 seconds).
> * Physical Damage Reduction from [Armour](/wiki/Armour "Armour") can no longer cause a hit to deal 0 damage. This is mostly targeted at preventing cases where multi-hitting player skills could deal 0 damage to armoured monsters at very low levels. In these cases, the hit will now deal 1 damage.
> * [Igniting](/wiki/Ignite "Ignite") [aura](/wiki/Aura "Aura") effects, including [Ignited Ground](/wiki/Ignited_Ground "Ignited Ground"), no longer apply infinite ignites. Instead they apply regular ignites with standard duration, and will reapply them after they expire the next time the aura applies [flammability](/wiki/Flammability "Flammability") to that target (the same as if Ignite had been removed from the target).
> * When [Parrying](/wiki/Parry "Parry"), you now hit all enemies in an area in front of you, in addition to the enemy who instigated the Parry.
> * ![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Item_inventory_icon.png/16px-Item_inventory_icon.png)[Parry](/wiki/Parry "Parry")Parry[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Physical](/wiki/Physical_%28gem_tag%29 "Physical (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Channelling](/wiki/Channelling_%28gem_tag%29 "Channelling (gem tag)")
>   Level: *1*
>   Attack Time: *0.75 sec*
>   Critical Strike Chance: *5.00%*
>   Attack Damage: *65% of base*Requires: *[Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler")*Ready your [Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler") to parry the next [Strike](/wiki/Strike "Strike") or [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") that would [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") you, [Blocking](/wiki/Block "Block") the [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") and retaliating with a quick sweep that leaves enemies off balance, causing them to take massively increased [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") damage for a short duration. Parrying causes you to accumulate [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup. You cannot [Evade](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") a [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") you could parry, but [Evasion](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") instead grants an equal chance to avoid this [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup.Can't be [Evaded](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion")
>   400% more [Stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") buildup
>   Can [Block](/wiki/Block "Block") [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") from enemies within 1 metre
>   Can [Block](/wiki/Block "Block") [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") from enemies within 1.5 metres
>   [Parried Debuff](/wiki/Parried_Debuff "Parried Debuff") makes targets take 50% more [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Damage
>   [Parried](/wiki/Parried "Parried") [Debuff](/wiki/Debuff "Debuff") duration is 2 seconds
>   3 to 4 Added [Physical](/wiki/Physical "Physical") Damage per 5 [Evasion Rating](/wiki/Evasion_Rating "Evasion Rating") on [Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler")Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/c/c7/Parry_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AParry_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Item_inventory_icon.png/78px-Item_inventory_icon.png) now always hits the enemy you parried, regardless of distance.
> * [Sprinting](/wiki/Sprint "Sprint") no longer prevents [heavy stun](/wiki/Heavy_stun "Heavy stun") buildup decay.
> * [Totem](/wiki/Totem "Totem") Placement speed now also scales the speed at which Totems emerge.
>
> ### Ascendancy Changes
>
> All Skills granted by an Ascendency are now automatically activated when granted (some previously required the player to manually activate them).
>
> #### [Deadeye](/wiki/Deadeye "Deadeye")
>
> * [Wind Ward](/wiki/Wind_Ward "Wind Ward") has been Removed.
> * [Bullseye](/wiki/Bullseye "Bullseye") now requires [Called Shots](/wiki/Called_Shots_%28passive%29 "Called Shots (passive)"). Bullseye now applies 10 Critical Weakness (previously 5).
> * Added a new [Mirage Deadeye](/wiki/Mirage_Deadeye_%28passive%29 "Mirage Deadeye (passive)") Ascendancy Passive Skill which grants the [![](/images/thumb/3/3b/Mirage_Deadeye_skill_icon.png/14px-Mirage_Deadeye_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Mirage_Deadeye "Mirage Deadeye")[Mirage Deadeye](/wiki/Mirage_Deadeye "Mirage Deadeye") Meta Skill. Mirage Deadeye: While active, firing a Ranged Attack Projectile will create a Mirage that uses socketed Ranged Attacks for a short duration, then vanishes. You cannot create another Mirage for a short time after initially creating one.
>
> #### [Pathfinder](/wiki/Pathfinder "Pathfinder")
>
> * [Contagious Contamination](/wiki/Contagious_Contamination "Contagious Contamination") has been Removed.
> * [Practical Remedies](/wiki/Practical_Remedies "Practical Remedies") has been Removed.
> * [Running Assault](/wiki/Running_Assault "Running Assault") now also grants Cannot be Heavy Stunned while Sprinting.
> * Added a new [Path Seeker](/wiki/Path_Seeker "Path Seeker") multi-choice Ascendancy Passive Skill with the following choices: [Path of the Warrior](/wiki/Path_of_the_Warrior "Path of the Warrior") - Can Allocate Passives from the Warrior's starting point, [Path of the Sorceress](/wiki/Path_of_the_Sorceress "Path of the Sorceress") - Can Allocate Passives from the Sorceress's starting point. Each choice also Grants 4 Passive Skill Points.
> * [Traveller's Wisdom](/wiki/Traveller%27s_Wisdom "Traveller's Wisdom") now requires Path Seeker. Traveller's Wisdom now instead grants Attribute Passive Skills offer additional Options:
>   + 5% increased Damage
>   + 5% increased Global Defences
>   + 5% increased Cost Efficiency
>
> #### [Amazon](/wiki/Amazon "Amazon")
>
> * [Elemental Surge](/wiki/Elemental_Surge_%28passive%29 "Elemental Surge (passive)") reworked:
>   + Grants Skill: [![](/images/thumb/6/69/Elemental_Surge_skill_icon.png/14px-Elemental_Surge_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Elemental_Surge "Elemental Surge")[Elemental Surge](/wiki/Elemental_Surge "Elemental Surge")
>   + Now provides When you consume a Charge Trigger Elemental Surge to gain 3 Lightning Surges.
> * [Surging Avatar](/wiki/Surging_Avatar "Surging Avatar") reworked:
>   + Now provides When you consume a Charge, Trigger Elemental Surge to instead gain 2 Cold, Lightning and Fire Surges.
>
> #### [Ritualist](/wiki/Ritualist "Ritualist")
>
> * [Ritual Sacrifice](/wiki/Ritual_Sacrifice "Ritual Sacrifice") Stolen Modifier duration is 82-120 seconds from Gem level 1-20 (previously 15-19.75). Quality is now +20 seconds to Stolen Modifier duration (previously +2).
> * [Corrupted Lifeforce](/wiki/Corrupted_Lifeforce "Corrupted Lifeforce") now also has You deal 15% more Damage to Enemies Affected by [![](/images/thumb/5/5d/Blood_Boil_skill_icon.png/14px-Blood_Boil_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Blood_Boil "Blood Boil")[Blood Boil](/wiki/Blood_Boil "Blood Boil").
>
> #### [Warbringer](/wiki/Warbringer "Warbringer")
>
> * [Imploding Impacts](/wiki/Imploding_Impacts "Imploding Impacts") now also grants Fully Broken Armour you inflict increases all Damage Taken from Hits instead.
> * The [Ancestral Warhorn](/wiki/Ancestral_Warhorn/edit?redlink=1 "Ancestral Warhorn (page does not exist)") minion summoned by Warbringer's [Answered Call](/wiki/Answered_Call "Answered Call") notable now more consistently hits close-up enemies with the second part of its slam attack.
>
> #### [Titan](/wiki/Titan "Titan")
>
> * [Surprising Strength](/wiki/Surprising_Strength "Surprising Strength") has been removed.
> * [Crushing Impacts](/wiki/Crushing_Impacts "Crushing Impacts") now also Grants 25% more Damage against Heavy Stunned Enemies.
> * Added a new [Mountain Splitter](/wiki/Mountain_Splitter "Mountain Splitter") Ascendancy Passive Skill which grants Every Third Slam Skill that doesn't create Fissures which you use yourself causes 3 additional Aftershocks ahead and to each side of the initial area. Requires [Crushing Impacts](/wiki/Crushing_Impacts "Crushing Impacts").
>
> #### [Smith of Kitava](/wiki/Smith_of_Kitava "Smith of Kitava")
>
> * Each Notable connected to the [Smith's Masterwork](/wiki/Smith%27s_Masterwork "Smith's Masterwork") Notable now grants +200 to Armour in addition to its other bonuses.
> * [Padded Plates](/wiki/Padded_Plates "Padded Plates") has been removed.
> * [Lead Lining](/wiki/Lead_Lining "Lead Lining") has been removed.
> * [Heavy Bracing](/wiki/Heavy_Bracing "Heavy Bracing") has been removed.
> * Added [Kitavan Imprint](/wiki/Kitavan_Imprint "Kitavan Imprint") in place of Padded Plates, which causes your Body Armour to grant 60% increased Glory Generation.
> * Added [Spiked Plates](/wiki/Spiked_Plates "Spiked Plates") in place of Lead Lining, which causes your Body Armour to grant 100% increased Thorns Damage.
> * Added [Tribute to Utula](/wiki/Tribute_to_Utula "Tribute to Utula") in place of Heavy Bracing, which causes your Body Armour to grant 30% increased Spirit.
> * [Internal Layer](/wiki/Internal_Layer "Internal Layer") now reduces Critical Damage taken by 100% (previously 50%).
> * [Heatproofing](/wiki/Heatproofing "Heatproofing") now causes your Body Armour to grant the bonus of being Unaffected by all Damaging Ailments (previously just ignite).
> * The [![](/images/thumb/e/eb/Fire_Spell_on_Melee_Hit_skill_icon.png/14px-Fire_Spell_on_Melee_Hit_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Fire_Spell_on_Hit "Fire Spell on Hit")[Fire Spell on Melee Hit](/wiki/Fire_Spell_on_Hit "Fire Spell on Hit") Skill granted by [Heat of the Forge](/wiki/Heat_of_the_Forge "Heat of the Forge") on Smith of Kitava now costs no mana when triggering Socketed Spells. It also now gains 10% increased Damage per Level, up to 200% increased Damage at gem level 20.
> * The [![](/images/thumb/d/d5/Temper_Weapon_skill_icon.png/14px-Temper_Weapon_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Temper_Weapon "Temper Weapon")[Temper Weapon](/wiki/Temper_Weapon "Temper Weapon") Skill granted by [Against the Anvil](/wiki/Against_the_Anvil "Against the Anvil") on Smith of Kitava now costs no mana. The Combust triggered by it's Empowered Attacks now deal 25% more Damage at all Levels and has a base radius of 3 Metres (previously 2.5 metres).
> * The [![](/images/thumb/8/8a/Manifest_Weapon_skill_icon.png/14px-Manifest_Weapon_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Manifest_Weapon "Manifest Weapon")[Manifest Weapon](/wiki/Manifest_Weapon "Manifest Weapon") Skill granted by [Living Weapon](/wiki/Living_Weapon "Living Weapon") on Smith of Kitava now changes target less frequently, and thus spends more time actively attacking. Additionally:
>   + As a Mace, now has a cooldown of 6 seconds (from 10 seconds) for its Slam Skill.
>   + As a Quarterstaff, now has a cooldown of 6 seconds (from 10 seconds) on its Sweep Skill.
>   + As a Spear, fixed a bug where the damage dealt while it was Dashing towards enemies didn't cover the full distance of the Dash.
>
> #### [Infernalist](/wiki/Infernalist "Infernalist")
>
> * [Seething Body](/wiki/Seething_Body "Seething Body") no longer grants While on High Infernal Flame, you and Allies in your Presence Gain 50% of Damage as Fire Damage. Seething Body now grants Gain Elemental Archon when you cast a Spell while on High Infernal Flame. Elemental Archon does not expire while on High Infernal Flame. Lose Elemental Archon on reaching maximum Infernal Flame.
>
> #### [Blood Mage](/wiki/Blood_Mage "Blood Mage")
>
> * [Whispers of the Flesh](/wiki/Whispers_of_the_Flesh "Whispers of the Flesh") now also grants Targets Cursed by you have 100% reduced Life Regeneration Rate.
>
> #### [Stormweaver](/wiki/Stormweaver "Stormweaver")
>
> * [Refracted Infusion](/wiki/Refracted_Infusion "Refracted Infusion") now grants: When collecting an Elemental Infusion, gain another different Elemental Infusion (previously 50% chance).
> * [Storm's Recollection](/wiki/Storm%27s_Recollection "Storm's Recollection") now also grants Remnants can be collected from 50% further away.
> * [Multiplying Squalls](/wiki/Multiplying_Squalls "Multiplying Squalls") now grants +2 to Limit of Elemental Skills (previously 1).
>
> #### [Chronomancer](/wiki/Chronomancer "Chronomancer")
>
> * [![](/images/thumb/6/64/Inevitable_Agony_skill_icon.png/14px-Inevitable_Agony_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Inevitable_Agony "Inevitable Agony")[Inevitable Agony](/wiki/Inevitable_Agony "Inevitable Agony") granted by [Inevitability](/wiki/Inevitability "Inevitability") has been updated:
>   + Now ignores the Curse Limit.
>   + Now causes Cursed Targets to take 50% of Hit Damage dealt to them while Cursed again when Curse expires (previously 20% at Gem level 1, scaling to 33% by Gem level 20).
>
> #### [Gemling Legionnaire](/wiki/Gemling_Legionnaire "Gemling Legionnaire")
>
> * [Thaumaturgical Infusion](/wiki/Thaumaturgical_Infusion "Thaumaturgical Infusion") now grants: +1% to Maximum Cold Resistance per 3 Blue Support Gems Socketed (previously 4). +1% to Maximum Fire Resistance per 3 Red Support Gems Socketed (previously 4). +1% to Maximum Lightning Resistance per 3 Green Support Gems Socketed (previously 4).
> * Thaumaturgical Dynamism granted by [Advanced Thaumaturgy](/wiki/Advanced_Thaumaturgy "Advanced Thaumaturgy") Notable Passive Skill now generates a Charge once every five seconds (previously once every eight seconds).
>
> #### [Tactician](/wiki/Tactician "Tactician")
>
> * The [![](/images/thumb/a/aa/Supporting_Fire_skill_icon.png/14px-Supporting_Fire_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Supporting_Fire "Supporting Fire")[Supporting Fire](/wiki/Supporting_Fire "Supporting Fire") Skill granted by [Unleash Hell!](/wiki/Unleash_Hell%21 "Unleash Hell!") Notable Passive Skill has been updated: Command: Death From Above Cooldown is now 20 seconds (previously 40). Now fires a Volley every 0.75 seconds (previously every 2 seconds). Now fires 6 total Volleys (previously 4). Now has 14 metre width (previously 7.5 metre width). Attack Damage is now 763% (previously 1140%).
> * [Strategic Embankments](/wiki/Strategic_Embankments "Strategic Embankments") Notable Passive Skill has been updated:

> #### [Witchhunter](/wiki/Witchhunter "Witchhunter")
>
> * [Witchbane](/wiki/Witchbane "Witchbane") now has Enemies have Maximum Concentration equal to 30% of their Maximum Life (previously 40%). This is a buff.
> * [Ceremonial Ablution](/wiki/Ceremonial_Ablution "Ceremonial Ablution") now instead grants [![](/images/thumb/3/39/Sorcery_Ward_skill_icon.png/14px-Sorcery_Ward_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Sorcery_Ward "Sorcery Ward")[Sorcery Ward](/wiki/Sorcery_Ward "Sorcery Ward") also protects against Physical and Chaos Damage.
>
> #### [Invoker](/wiki/Invoker "Invoker")
>
> * [...and Protect me from harm](/wiki/...and_Protect_me_from_Harm "...and Protect me from Harm"): Now grants 35% less Evasion Rating (previously 50% less).
> * [The Soul Springs Eternal](/wiki/The_Soul_Springs_Eternal "The Soul Springs Eternal") now additionally grants Meta Skills have 50% increased Spirit Reservation Efficiency.
> * [![](/images/thumb/a/ad/Unbound_Avatar_skill_icon.png/14px-Unbound_Avatar_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Unbound_Avatar "Unbound Avatar")[Unbound Avatar](/wiki/Unbound_Avatar "Unbound Avatar") Skill granted by [...and I Shall Rage](/wiki/...and_I_Shall_Rage "...and I Shall Rage") has been updated:
>   + Now has a cooldown of 12 seconds.
>   + Gain Unbound Fury when you inflict an Elemental Ailment with a Hit on an Enemy, no longer has 'No more than once every 0.2 seconds for each type of Ailment'.
>   + Shocking and Igniting now grant 1 Unbound Fury (previously 2).
>
> #### [Acolyte of Chayula](/wiki/Acolyte_of_Chayula "Acolyte of Chayula")
>
> * [Embrace the Darkness](/wiki/Embrace_the_Darkness "Embrace the Darkness") now gives +10 to maximum Darkness per Level (previously +8).
> * The [![](/images/thumb/3/31/Into_the_Breach_skill_icon.png/14px-Into_the_Breach_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Into_the_Breach "Into the Breach")[Into the Breach](/wiki/Into_the_Breach "Into the Breach") Skill granted by [Waking Dream](/wiki/Waking_Dream "Waking Dream")' Red Flames now Leech 15% Life (previously 7%).
> * The Into the Breach Skill granted by Waking Dream' Blue Flames now Leech 15% Mana (previously 7%).
> * The Into the Breach Skill granted by Waking Dream' Purple Flames now last 8 seconds (previously 5 seconds).
> * The Into the Breach Skill granted by Waking Dream' Flames are now created closer to the Player.
> * [Choice of Power](/wiki/Choice_of_Power "Choice of Power"), [Choice of Life](/wiki/Choice_of_Life "Choice of Life") and [Choice of Mana](/wiki/Choice_of_Mana "Choice of Mana") now all also grant 50% increased effect of Remnants, and 50% increased Remnant Pickup Range.
> * The [![](/images/thumb/6/69/Void_Illusion_skill_icon.png/14px-Void_Illusion_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/Void_Illusion "Void Illusion")[Void Illusion](/wiki/Void_Illusion "Void Illusion") Skill granted by [Grasp of the Void](/wiki/Grasp_of_the_Void "Grasp of the Void") now has a Cooldown of 4 seconds at all gem levels (previously 6-4).
> * The Void Illusion Skill granted by Grasp of the Void now deals 350-1268% Attack Damage at Gem levels 1-20 (previously 185-670%).
> * The Void Illusion Skill granted by Grasp of the Void now has 3 Cooldown Charges (previously 1).
>
> ### Passive Skill Tree Changes
>
> With the addition of the Druid and other new game mechanics we've added passive support for these throughout the Passive Skill Tree. There are many new clusters, mostly in the Druid area of the tree, and many existing Passive Skills have been updated. These changes may result in your existing passive tree being forcefully refunded if you had allocated nodes around the areas where the layout changed.
>
> * Added more than 250 new Passive Skills to the Druid side of the passive tree.
> * The values of [Flammability](/wiki/Flammability "Flammability") Magnitude on the Passive Tree have been increased massively.
> * All instances of gaining Flame, Ice and Lightning [Archon](/wiki/Archon "Archon") have been changed to gain Elemental Archon, to better support builds using multiple Elements. Archon related passives on the tree have been adjusted accordingly and condensed.
> * The [Hollow Palm Technique](/wiki/Hollow_Palm_Technique "Hollow Palm Technique") Keystone now Grants 1% more Attack Speed per 75 Item Evasion Rating on Equipped Armour Items (previously 25). Base unarmed attack time is now 1.65 attacks per second (previously 1.4).
> * The [Walker of the Wilds](/wiki/Walker_of_the_Wilds "Walker of the Wilds") Keystone has been removed from the passive tree and its effects have been moved onto a newly added Lineage Support.
> * The [Elemental Equilibrium](/wiki/Elemental_Equilibrium "Elemental Equilibrium") Keystone now grants Cold Infusion Remnants you create are instead Fire, Fire Infusion Remnants you create are instead Lightning, Lightning Infusion Remnants you create are instead Cold.
> * The [Crimson Assault](/wiki/Crimson_Assault "Crimson Assault") Keystone Passive Skill now also grants 50% more Magnitude of Bleeding you inflict.
> * Passives that granted reduced [Movement Speed](/wiki/Movement_Speed "Movement Speed") Penalty from using Skills while moving on the Passive Tree have had their values lowered. More passives on the tree now grant the stat to make up for some of this.
> * Added 3 new Attack [Area of Effect](/wiki/Area_of_Effect "Area of Effect") Clusters to the [Monk](/wiki/Monk "Monk") part of the Passive Tree.
> * Added two [projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") speed clusters to the Passive Tree in the [Mercenary](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") section.
> * Added a new [bow](/wiki/Bow "Bow") cluster and modified a projectile cluster in the ranger section of the tree, granting Surpassing chance to fire an additional Arrow.
> * Added a new cluster between Witch and Monk called [Remnant Attraction](/wiki/Remnant_Attraction/edit?redlink=1 "Remnant Attraction (page does not exist)").
> * [Principal Infusion](/wiki/Principal_Infusion "Principal Infusion") now has Remnants can be collected from 30% further away (previously 20%).
> * The [Grand Tribute](/wiki/Grand_Tribute "Grand Tribute") notable from the ![](/images/thumb/1/10/Undying_Hate_inventory_icon.png/16px-Undying_Hate_inventory_icon.png)[Heart of the Well](/wiki/Undying_Hate "Undying Hate")Undying Hate
>   Timeless JewelLimited to: *1 Historic*
>   Radius: *Very Large*Glorifying the defilement of (79-30977) souls in tribute to (Amanamu-Ulaman-Kurgal-Tecrod-Kulemak)
>   Passives in radius are Conquered by the Abyssals
>   Desecration makes this item Unstable
>   Historic
>   <Can gain 0-4 custom [Desecrated Modifiers](/wiki/Desecrated_Modifier "Desecrated Modifier")> (Hidden)They believed themselves driven by necessity,
>   but that desperation made them monstrous.Place into an allocated Jewel Socket on the Passive Skill Tree. Right click to remove from the Socket.
>   Can be Desecrated 4 Times.
>   Desecration makes the item unstable.![](/images/thumb/1/10/Undying_Hate_inventory_icon.png/78px-Undying_Hate_inventory_icon.png) [*[sic](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sic "wikipedia:sic")*] Unique Jewel now has [Remnants](/wiki/Remnant "Remnant") can be collected from 80% further away if you have at least 100 Tribute (previously 50%).
> * Small nodes on the passive tree that grant Remnant Pickup Range now grant Remnants can be collected from 20% further away (previously 15%).
> * Small nodes on Ascendancies that grant Remnant Pickup Range now grant Remnants can be collected from 25% further away (previously 20%).
> * The small passive connected to the [Invigorating Grandeur](/wiki/Invigorating_Grandeur/edit?redlink=1 "Invigorating Grandeur (page does not exist)") and [Everlasting Glory](/wiki/Everlasting_Glory/edit?redlink=1 "Everlasting Glory (page does not exist)") notables now grants 20% increased [Presence](/wiki/Presence "Presence") Area of Effect instead of Skills a chance to not consume Glory.
> * The [Pure Power](/wiki/Pure_Power "Pure Power") notable no longer grants 2% increased Lightning Damage per 10 Intelligence. Instead it now grants 10% more Maximum Lightning Damage.
> * [Wild Storm](/wiki/Wild_Storm "Wild Storm") no longer grants 15% more Maximum Lightning Damage. It instead now grants: Gain 4% of Damage as Extra Lightning Damage, Gain 4% of Damage as Extra Cold Damage and +10 to Dexterity.
> * Renamed Tandem Assault passive tree node to [Hunting Companion](/wiki/Hunting_Companion/edit?redlink=1 "Hunting Companion (page does not exist)"), with no change to functionality.
> * Changed the stats on several small passive tree nodes around the [Inspiring Ally](/wiki/Inspiring_Ally/edit?redlink=1 "Inspiring Ally (page does not exist)"), [Hunting Companion](/wiki/Hunting_Companion/edit?redlink=1 "Hunting Companion (page does not exist)"), [Sic 'Em](/wiki/Sic_%27Em/edit?redlink=1 "Sic 'Em (page does not exist)"), and [Nourishing Ally](/wiki/Nourishing_Ally/edit?redlink=1 "Nourishing Ally (page does not exist)") nodes. [Companion](/wiki/Companion "Companion") cluster small passive skills now generally no longer grant both Companions deal increased Damage and increased Damage while your Companion is in your Presence.
> * Added some additional ![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Item_inventory_icon.png/16px-Item_inventory_icon.png)[Parry](/wiki/Parry "Parry")Parry[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Physical](/wiki/Physical_%28gem_tag%29 "Physical (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Channelling](/wiki/Channelling_%28gem_tag%29 "Channelling (gem tag)")
>   Level: *1*
>   Attack Time: *0.75 sec*
>   Critical Strike Chance: *5.00%*
>   Attack Damage: *65% of base*Requires: *[Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler")*Ready your [Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler") to parry the next [Strike](/wiki/Strike "Strike") or [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") that would [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") you, [Blocking](/wiki/Block "Block") the [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") and retaliating with a quick sweep that leaves enemies off balance, causing them to take massively increased [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") damage for a short duration. Parrying causes you to accumulate [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup. You cannot [Evade](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") a [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") you could parry, but [Evasion](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") instead grants an equal chance to avoid this [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup.Can't be [Evaded](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion")
>   400% more [Stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") buildup
>   Can [Block](/wiki/Block "Block") [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") from enemies within 1 metre
>   Can [Block](/wiki/Block "Block") [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") from enemies within 1.5 metres
>   [Parried Debuff](/wiki/Parried_Debuff "Parried Debuff") makes targets take 50% more [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Damage
>   [Parried](/wiki/Parried "Parried") [Debuff](/wiki/Debuff "Debuff") duration is 2 seconds
>   3 to 4 Added [Physical](/wiki/Physical "Physical") Damage per 5 [Evasion Rating](/wiki/Evasion_Rating "Evasion Rating") on [Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler")Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/c/c7/Parry_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AParry_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Item_inventory_icon.png/78px-Item_inventory_icon.png)-related passive nodes to the tree.
> * Made changes to some existing Parry-related passive nodes, including additional Parry Debuff Magnitude.
> * [Falcon Dive](/wiki/Falcon_Dive "Falcon Dive") now grants 1% Attack Speed per 400 Accuracy Rating, up to 20%. The node now grants 4% increased attack speed as well.
> * Added two clusters with increased ailment chance to the [Ranger](/wiki/Ranger "Ranger") and [Monk](/wiki/Monk "Monk") sections of the tree.
> * [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Area passive skills on the Passive Tree have been halved, now granting 10% Curse Area of Effect (previously 20%). The [Zone of Control](/wiki/Zone_of_Control/edit?redlink=1 "Zone of Control (page does not exist)") Notable skill now grants 20% increased Curse Area of Effect (previously 40%) but also grants 10% increased Curse Magnitudes (previously 8%). The Curse Area small passives on the [Lich](/wiki/Lich "Lich") and [Abyssal Lich](/wiki/Abyssal_Lich "Abyssal Lich") now grant 15% increased Curse Area (previously 25%).
>

>   Tier: *5*Support Requirements: *+5 Str*Supports [Slam](/wiki/Slam "Slam") Skills. Supported Skills create [Hazardous](/wiki/Hazard "Hazard") Brambles on the ground that activate after a duration. >
>   Brambles
>   Cooldown Time: 0.15 s
>   Hazardous thorns damage and Maim enemies with which they come in contact.
>   Attack Damage of this skill is 35% of Default Attack Damage
>   Increases and reductions to Thorns Damage apply to Hit Damage with this skill
>   Maim on Hit
>   80% less damage if destroyed within 0.5 seconds by something other than you
>   Bramble radius is 1 metre
>   Bramble duration is 8 secondsPlace into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. >   [Curses](/wiki/Curse "Curse") inflicted by Supported Skills are reflected back to you
>   Supported Skills have 20% less [Curse Effect](/wiki/Curse "Curse")Such was her seductive power, every noble in the court fell
>   over themselves to do her bidding. Winning a single glance
>   away from her mirror meant more than their lives.Place into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. > * [Living Lightning](/wiki/Living_Lightning "Living Lightning")'s living lightnings' Attacks now deal the same amount of damage for each Hit in the Chain (previously erroneously dealing less damage per subsequent Hit in the Chain).
> * ![](/images/thumb/c/c4/Living_Lightning_I_inventory_icon.png/16px-Living_Lightning_I_inventory_icon.png)[Living Lightning II](/wiki/Living_Lightning_II "Living Lightning II")Living Lightning II[Support](/wiki/Support_%28gem_tag%29 "Support (gem tag)"), [Minion](/wiki/Minion_%28gem_tag%29 "Minion (gem tag)"), [Trigger](/wiki/Trigger_%28gem_tag%29 "Trigger (gem tag)"), [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning_%28gem_tag%29 "Lightning (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)")
>   Category: *Living Lightning*
>   Tier: *4*Support Requirements: *+5 Int*Supports Skills which cause [Damaging Hits](/wiki/Damaging_Hit "Damaging Hit"). Living Lightning [Minions](/wiki/Minion "Minion") are created when dealing [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") damage with Supported Skills - bundles of living electricity that target nearby enemies with [Chaining](/wiki/Chain "Chain") [Attacks](/wiki/Attack "Attack"). Enemies will not directly engage these [Minions](/wiki/Minion "Minion"), and can pass through them. Does not modify skills used by [Minions](/wiki/Minion "Minion").[Trigger](/wiki/Trigger "Trigger") Living Lightning on dealing [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") Damage with Supported Skill
>
>   Living Lightning
>   Cooldown Time: (0.20 s (5 Times))
>   Minions from this skill have 1% increased Attack Speed per 10 of your Dexterity
>   Minions from this skill have 1% increased Damage per 5 of your Strength
>   This Skill is Triggered on dealing Lightning Damage with Supported Skill
>   Creates 1 Minion
>   Level of Minions is based on Level of Triggering Skill
>   Minion duration is 30 seconds
>   Limit 8 Minions
>   Minions convert 100% of Physical damage to Lightning damage
>   Minions Attack every 0.14 seconds
>   Minions disperse after 3 AttacksPlace into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. > * [Enraged Warcry](/wiki/Enraged_Warcry "Enraged Warcry") and [Rageforged](/wiki/Rageforged "Rageforged") Supports are now treated as spending Rage.
> * [Upheaval](/wiki/Upheaval "Upheaval") and [Branching Fissure](/wiki/Branching_Fissure "Branching Fissure") Supports are no longer restricted to melee attacks. They can now support any skill which creates fissures.

>   Category: *Cursed Ground*Requires Level *65*
>   Support Requirements: *+5 Int*Supports [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Skills. Supported [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Skills create [Hazardous](/wiki/Hazard "Hazard") areas which explode when Enemies enter them, [Cursing](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Enemies and dealing [Chaos](/wiki/Chaos "Chaos") Damage.Support
>   Supported Skills create [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground
>   Enemies on the [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground from a Supported Skill are [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") while within it
>   [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground created by Supported Skills counts as a [Hazard](/wiki/Hazard "Hazard")
>   Maximum 2 areas of [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground
>   [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground created by Supported Skills triggers Doedre's Dark Design when Enemies enter
>
>   Doedre's Dark Design
>   Explodes and deals Chaos Damage when an Enemy enters the area, applying the supported Curse on Hit.>
>   Deals 7 to 13 Chaos Damage
>   Explosion applies Supported Curse for 3 seconds on Hit
>
> Explosion radius is equal to that of the Cursed Ground
> "Let the meat show us the way. Hail the meat, praise the
> meat. The meat is both debasement and divinity alike. The
> meat shall lead us down the path to true enlightenment."Place into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. You cannot have multiple Support Gems of the same Category socketed within one Skill.![](/images/thumb/0/0c/Doedre%27s_Undoing_inventory_icon.png/78px-Doedre%27s_Undoing_inventory_icon.png) by changing it from scaling off Intellgence to instead scale based on the Supported Curses Level. This opens up the build without having to be Intelligence stacking.

This change has been made to make Frozen Locus stronger with things that scale off Ice Crystal life, while keeping the amount of damage to destroy the crystal from both players and monsters roughly the same. Frozen Locus Ice Crystal has 27-9536 maximum Life (from 430-1364).
> * ![](/images/thumb/f/f4/Gathering_Storm_inventory_icon.png/16px-Gathering_Storm_inventory_icon.png)[Gathering Storm](/wiki/Gathering_Storm "Gathering Storm")Gathering Storm[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning_%28gem_tag%29 "Lightning (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Channelling](/wiki/Channelling_%28gem_tag%29 "Channelling (gem tag)"), [Travel](/wiki/Travel_%28gem_tag%29 "Travel (gem tag)")
>   Tier: *13*
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(7-53) Mana per second*
>   Attack Damage: *(120-435)% of base*Requires: *[Quarterstaff](/wiki/Quarterstaff "Quarterstaff")*Flip backward and [Channel](/wiki/Channelling "Channelling") to charge your [Quarterstaff](/wiki/Quarterstaff "Quarterstaff") with [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning"). Releasing dashes towards the target location, damaging enemies along the way. Releasing with [Perfect Timing](/wiki/Perfect_Timing "Perfect Timing") performs a [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning")-assisted dash that releases shockwaves from enemies you dash through and leaves a trail of [Shocked Ground](/wiki/Shocked_Ground "Shocked Ground") in your wake. This skill cannot be [Ancestrally Boosted](/wiki/Ancestrally_Boosted "Ancestrally Boosted").[Converts](/wiki/Damage_conversion "Damage conversion") 20% of [Physical](/wiki/Physical "Physical") damage to [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") damage
>   +0.8 seconds to Total [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Time
>   +10 to [Melee](/wiki/Melee "Melee") [Strike](/wiki/Strike "Strike") RangeSkills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/3/3d/Gathering_Storm_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AGathering_Storm_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/f/f4/Gathering_Storm_inventory_icon.png/78px-Gathering_Storm_inventory_icon.png): Perfect Timing window has been increased. Now has a much higher dash range. Shockwave now has Maximum 20 shockwaves per use (previously 8). Quality now grants Maximum +8 shockwaves per use (previously 2).

Quality now grants 20% more Ignite duration (previously ignite magnitude). Now gains 7-2 milliseconds of fuel per Mana spent (previously 10-5). >    *[Minions](/wiki/Minion "Minion") have (1-20)% increased effect of [Rage](/wiki/Rage "Rage")**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/0/0a/Skeletal_Reaver_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3ASkeletal_Reaver_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/a/a7/Skeletal_Reaver_inventory_icon.png/78px-Skeletal_Reaver_inventory_icon.png): Now gain 6% increased attack speed per 2 rage, previously this was described on the gem but not functional.

Hitting such an enemy will cause your arrow to release a damaging shockwave and [Chain](/wiki/Chain "Chain") towards nearby targets, with those [Chaining](/wiki/Chain "Chain") [Hits](/wiki/Hit "Hit") also releasing a shockwave. After the final [Chain](/wiki/Chain "Chain"), the arrow lodges into the ground as a Lightning Rod. [Consumes](/wiki/Effect_Consumption "Effect Consumption") [Shock](/wiki/Shock "Shock") from enemies it [Hits](/wiki/Hit "Hit"), but not [Electrocution](/wiki/Electrocution "Electrocution").Projectile

>   Attack Damage: (140-507)% of base

Shockchain Arrow no longer releases secondary beams that continue to split. Instead, the initial projectile now consumes Shock to create a Chaining secondary projectile, which creates a Lightning Rod in the ground near its last target after its final chain. This secondary projectile does not consume Shock on targets hit. Shockwave now deals 293-507% of Attack damage at Gem levels 11-20 (previously 306-572%).

> * Perfidy now has 10-30% chance to Avoid Fire Damage from Hits, 10-30% chance to Avoid Cold Damage from Hits and 10-30% chance to Avoid Lightning Damage from Hits. This change does not affect existing items.

It now either generates with "Equipment has 100% reduced Attribute Requirements" or "Skill Gems have 100% reduced Attribute Requirements". It also now has no Attribute Requirements. These changes do not affect existing versions of the item.

> * Indigon now has "5-10% Increased Cost of Skills for Each 200 Total Mana Spent Recently" (previously 35-50%). Existing items can be updated using a Divine Orb.

> ### Item Changes
>
> * ![](/images/thumb/6/60/Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png/16px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png)[Omen of Homogenising Exaltation](/wiki/Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation "Omen of Homogenising Exaltation")Omen of Homogenising ExaltationStack Size: *10*While this item is active in your inventory your next
>   Exalted Orb will add a Modifier of the same
>   type as an existing Modifier on the ItemRight click this item in your inventory to set it to be active. This item is consumed when triggered.![](/images/thumb/6/60/Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png/78px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png) and the ![](/images/thumb/0/0b/Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation_inventory_icon.png/16px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation_inventory_icon.png)[Omen of Homogenising Coronation](/wiki/Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation "Omen of Homogenising Coronation")Omen of Homogenising CoronationStack Size: *10*While this item is active in your inventory your next
>   Regal Orb will add a Modifier of the same
>   type as an existing Modifier on the ItemRight click this item in your inventory to set it to be active. Existing items are still functional.
> * Rune Sockets have been renamed to [Augment Sockets](/wiki/Augment_Socket "Augment Socket").
> * Non-[jewel](/wiki/Jewel "Jewel") items that go into Augment Sockets have been renamed from Socketables to [Augments](/wiki/Augment "Augment").
> * Existing Augment Talismans have been renamed to [Idols](/wiki/Idol "Idol").
> * Existing items that have invalid Augment Sockets from the following Limit changes will be unable to be used until the Sockets are once again valid.

>   + "of Surplus" (25 - 50%)
>   + "of Splintering" (75 - 100%)
>   + "of Shards" (125 - 150%)
>   + "of Many" (175 - 200%)

> * Magnitude of Damaging Ailments [desecrated mod](/wiki/Desecrated_mod "Desecrated mod") on staves now rolls from 40 to 64 (previous 31 to 49). Existing items can be updated using a Divine Orb.
> * Spell Damage with Spells that cost life desecrated mod on Staves now rolls from 121 to 154 (previously 91 to 116).
> * [Foci](/wiki/Foci "Foci") can no longer roll the top 2 tiers of spell damage and specific damage modifiers.

>   [Bow](/wiki/Bow "Bow") or [Crossbow](/wiki/Crossbow "Crossbow"): (14-16)% increased [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") SpeedRight click this item then left click a Magic item to apply it.![](/images/thumb/f/fb/Greater_Essence_of_Haste_inventory_icon.png/78px-Greater_Essence_of_Haste_inventory_icon.png) now adds (14-16)% increased Attack Speed to Bows and Crossbows, this is unchanged on Melee Weapons. Existing Items will not be affected by this change.
> * The ![](/images/thumb/e/ee/Perfect_Essence_of_Sorcery_inventory_icon.png/16px-Perfect_Essence_of_Sorcery_inventory_icon.png)[Perfect Essence of Sorcery](/wiki/Perfect_Essence_of_Sorcery "Perfect Essence of Sorcery")Perfect Essence of SorceryStack Size: *10*Removes a random modifier and augments a [Rare](/wiki/Rare "Rare") item with a new guaranteed modifier
>   [Wand](/wiki/Wand "Wand"): +3 to Level of all [Spell](/wiki/Spell "Spell") Skills
>   [Staff](/wiki/Staff "Staff"): +5 to Level of all [Spell](/wiki/Spell "Spell") SkillsRight click this item then left click a Rare item to apply it.![](/images/thumb/e/ee/Perfect_Essence_of_Sorcery_inventory_icon.png/78px-Perfect_Essence_of_Sorcery_inventory_icon.png) now cannot be applied to Foci. (Now only Wands and Staves).
> * The 'of the Mage' modifier (+1 to all Spell Skill levels) on Focus and [Amulet](/wiki/Amulet "Amulet") now has a level requirement of 10 (previously 5). Note, this will change the level Requirements of existing Items.
> * The 'of Coals' Modifier on Staves now grants +1 level to Fire Spells (from +2), this also applies to the equivalent Modifiers for Cold, Lightning, Chaos and Physical on Staves. Existing Items will not be affected by this change unless a Divine Orb is used.
> * The 'of Cinders' Modifier on Staves now grants +2 to level of Fire Spells (from +3), this also applies to the equivalent Modifiers for Cold, Lightning, Chaos and Physical on Staves. Existing Items will not be affected by this change unless a Divine Orb is used.
> * The 'of Flames' Modifier on Staves now grants +3 to +4 level of Fire Spells (from +4), this also applies to the equivalent Modifiers for Cold, Lightning, Chaos and Physical on Staves. Existing Items will not be affected by this change unless a Divine Orb is used.
> * The 'of the Mage' Modifier on Staves now grants +1 level to Spells (from +2). Existing Items will not be affected by this change unless a Divine Orb is used.
> * The 'of the Enchanter' Modifier on Staves now grants +2 to level of Fire Spells (from +3). Existing Items will not be affected by this change unless a Divine Orb is used.
> * The 'of the Evoker' Modifier on Staves now grants +3 to +4 level of Fire Spells (from +4). Existing Items will not be affected by this change unless a Divine Orb is used.
> * ![](/images/thumb/b/b1/Perfect_Essence_of_Battle_inventory_icon.png/16px-Perfect_Essence_of_Battle_inventory_icon.png)[Perfect Essence of Battle](/wiki/Perfect_Essence_of_Battle "Perfect Essence of Battle")Perfect Essence of BattleStack Size: *10*Removes a random modifier and augments a [Rare](/wiki/Rare "Rare") item with a new guaranteed modifier

>   Two Handed [Melee](/wiki/Melee "Melee") [Weapon](/wiki/Martial_Weapons "Martial Weapons") or [Crossbow](/wiki/Crossbow "Crossbow"): +5 to Level of all [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") SkillsRight click this item then left click a Rare item to apply it.![](/images/thumb/b/b1/Perfect_Essence_of_Battle_inventory_icon.png/78px-Perfect_Essence_of_Battle_inventory_icon.png) now grants +3 to Level of all attack skills on one handed melee weapons and bows (from +4). You can make your item worse with a Divine Orb.
> * Perfect Essence of Battle now grants +5 to Level of all attack skills on two handed melee weapons and crossbows (from +6). You can make your item worse with a Divine Orb.

Existing items can be updated using a Divine Orb. 80-94).

> * ![](/images/thumb/f/fd/Smuggler_Coat_inventory_icon.png/11px-Smuggler_Coat_inventory_icon.png)[Corsair Coat](/wiki/Corsair_Coat "Corsair Coat")Corsair CoatEvasion: *406*
>   Movement Speed: *-3.0%*Requires Level *80*, *121* Dex5% increased Movement Speed![](/images/thumb/f/fd/Smuggler_Coat_inventory_icon.png/156px-Smuggler_Coat_inventory_icon.png) now grants 5% increased Movement Speed instead of reduced Movement Speed Penalty from using Skills while moving.
> * ![](/images/thumb/4/42/Farrul%27s_Rune_of_Grace_inventory_icon.png/16px-Farrul%27s_Rune_of_Grace_inventory_icon.png)[Farrul's Rune of Grace](/wiki/Farrul%27s_Rune_of_Grace "Farrul's Rune of Grace")Farrul's Rune of GraceStack Size: *10*

> * ![](/images/thumb/0/09/Grip_of_Kulemak_inventory_icon.png/16px-Grip_of_Kulemak_inventory_icon.png)[Grip of Kulemak](/wiki/Grip_of_Kulemak "Grip of Kulemak")Grip of Kulemak

>   Let the Abyss coil within.![](/images/thumb/0/09/Grip_of_Kulemak_inventory_icon.png/78px-Grip_of_Kulemak_inventory_icon.png) can no longer roll reduced Movement Speed Penalty from using Skills while moving.
> * The Desecrated modifier on Amulets that granted Skills a chance to not consume Glory, now instead grants 20-30% chance for Skills to retain 40% of Glory on use. This affects existing items with these modifiers, and can be updated to the new values with a Divine Orb.
> * The Desecrated modifier granting reduced Movement Speed Penalty from using Skills has been removed.
> * Added a Relic Locker to every end-of-floor Reward room in the [Trial of the Sekhemas](/wiki/Trial_of_the_Sekhemas "Trial of the Sekhemas").
> * [Relic](/wiki/Relic "Relic") modifier "Light-footed" can no longer roll.
> * Relic modifier "Acrobatic" now grants "Traps deal (7-5)% reduced Damage" (previously 15-12%).
> * Relic modifier "Limber" now grants "Traps deal (10-8)% reduced Damage" (previously 15-12%).
> * ![](/images/thumb/b/b4/Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png/16px-Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png)[Rabbit Idol](/wiki/Rabbit_Idol "Rabbit Idol")Rabbit IdolStack Size: *10*Body Armours: 5% increased [Rarity of Items](/wiki/Rarity "Rarity") found

Once socketed it cannot be retrieved but can be replaced by other [Augment](/wiki/Augment "Augment") items.![](/images/thumb/b/b4/Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png/78px-Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png) now grants 5% increased Rarity of Items found (from 8%).
> * [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Area of Effect Mods on [Jewels](/wiki/Jewel "Jewel") have been reduced. Regular Jewels now grant 8-12% Curse Area of Effect (previously 15-25%) and Timeless Jewels now grant 3-6% (previously 6-12%).
>
> ### Endgame Changes
>
> [Maps](/wiki/Map "Map") no longer scale pack size as you increase in tier, they instead increase non-unique monster Effectiveness. Effectiveness grants monsters increased life, increased experience granted and increased quantity of items dropped. [Tablets](/wiki/Tablet "Tablet") now have a maximum of 4 modifiers. To unlock the ability to craft a tablet beyond 2 modifiers you need to have defeated [the Arbiter of Ash](/wiki/The_Arbiter_of_Ash "The Arbiter of Ash").
>
> * [Arbiter of Ash](/wiki/Arbiter_of_Ash "Arbiter of Ash") no longer drops a rare corrupted Tablet.
> * [The Arbiter of Ash](/wiki/The_Arbiter_of_Ash "The Arbiter of Ash") will now phase transition at a lower life threshold and will heal to full during the transition.
> * All Tablet modifiers that would roll on the generic "![](/images/thumb/7/75/Precursor_Tablet_inventory_icon.png/16px-Precursor_Tablet_inventory_icon.png)[Precursor Tablet](/wiki/Precursor_Tablet_%28generic%29 "Precursor Tablet (generic)")Precursor TabletAdds [Irradiated](/wiki/Irradiated "Irradiated") to a Map
>   10 uses remainingCan be used in a personal Map Device to add modifiers to a Map.![](/images/thumb/7/75/Precursor_Tablet_inventory_icon.png/78px-Precursor_Tablet_inventory_icon.png)" can now roll on all tablet basetypes. The following Tablet modifiers have been disabled:
>   + "Plundering" granting "4 to 10% increased Quantity of Items found in Map".
>   + "of the Pursuit" granting "Delirious Monsters Killed in Map provide 10 to 30% increased Reward Progress".
>   + "of Envy" granting "Delirium Encounters in affected Map have 8 to 24% chance to generate an additional Reward".
> * Added new Tablet modifiers:
>   + "Challenger's" which grants "7 to 11% increased Effectiveness of Monsters in your Maps".
>   + "of Contest" which grants "Unique Monsters in your Maps have 1 additional Rare Modifier".
> * Re-enabled the following modifier:
>   + "of Undertaking" which grants "Map has 1 to 2 additional random Modifiers".
> * The following Tablet modifiers have been buffed:
>   + "Collector's" now grants "18 to 30% increased Rarity of Items found in Map" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "Breeding" now grants "6 to 10% increased Pack Size in Map" (previously 4 to 10%).
>   + "Teeming" now grants "Map has 50 to 70% increased Magic Monsters" (previously 25 to 70%).
>   + "Brimming" now grants "Map has 25 to 40% increased number of Rare Monsters" (previously 15 to 40%).
>   + "Bountiful" now grants "25 to 40% increased Gold found in Map" (previously 15 to 40%).
>   + "Elevated" now grants "10 to 20% increased Experience gain in Map" (previously 5 to 20%).
>   + "Treasurer's" now grants "Map contains 2 to 3 additional Rare Chests" (previously 1 to 3).
>   + "of the Cartographer" now grants "30 to 50% increased Quantity of Waystones found in Map" (previously 20 to 50%).
>   + "of the Nemesis" now grants "Rare Monsters in Map have a 50 to 80% chance to have an additional Modifier" (previously 30 to 80%).
>   + "of Shrines" now grants "Map has 70 to 100% increased chance to contain Shrines" (previously 50 to 100%).
>   + "of Strongboxes" now grants "Map has 70 to 100% increased chance to contain Strongboxes" (previously 50 to 100%).
>   + "of the Essence" now grants "Map has 70 to 100% increased chance to contain Essences" (previously 50 to 100%).
>   + "of Spirits" now grants "Map has 70 to 100% increased chance to contain Azmeri Spirits" (previously 50 to 100%).
>   + "of the Exile" now grants "Map has 35 to 50% increased chance to contain Rogue Exiles" (previously 25 to 50%).
>   + "of the Summoning" now grants "Map has 35 to 50% increased chance to contain a Summoning Circle" (previously 25 to 50%).
>   + "of the Horde" now grants Breaches in Map spawn 40 to 70% increased Magic Monsters" (previously 25 to 70%).
>   + "of the Invasion" now grants Breaches in Map have 5 to 10% increased Monster density" (previously 4 to 10%).
>   + "of the Domain" now grants "15 to 30% increased Quantity of Breach Splinters dropped by Breach Monsters in Map" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Rupturing" now grants "Map has 6 to 10% chance to contain three additional Breaches" (previously 4 to 10%).
>   + "of Fissuring" now grants "Map has 15 to 30% chance to contain an additional Breach" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Verisium" now grants "15 to 30% increased quantity of Expedition Artifacts dropped by Monsters in Map" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of the Detonator" now grants "15 to 30% increased Expedition Explosive Placement Range in Map" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of the Demolition" now grants "15 to 30% increased Expedition Explosive Radius in Map" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Knowledge" now grants "15 to 30% increased Quantity of Expedition Logbooks dropped by Runic Monsters" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Ancient Fiends" now grants "25 to 40% increased number of Rare Expedition Monsters in Map" (previously 15 to 40%).
>   + "of Relics" now grants "12 to 18% increased Effect of Expedition Remnants in Map" (previously 6 to 18%).
>   + "of Runes" now grants "Map contains 15 to 30% increased number of Runic Monster Markers" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of the Simulacrum" now grants "15 to 30% increased Stack size of Simulacrum Splinters found in Map" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Madness" now grants "Delirium in Map increases 15 to 30% faster with distance from the mirror" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Persecution" now grants "Delirium Monsters in Map have 15 to 30% increased Pack Size" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Mirrors" now grants "Delirium Fog in Map spawns 15 to 30% increased Fracturing Mirrors" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Freeze Time" now grants "Slaying Rare Monsters in Map pauses the Delirium Mirror Timer for 3 to 5 seconds" (previously 2 to 5).
>   + "of Phobia" now grants "Delirium Encounters in Map are 15 to 30% more likely to spawn Unique Bosses" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Sacrifice" now grants "Monsters Sacrificed at Ritual Altars in Map grant 18 to 30% increased Tribute" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of the Appeal" now grants "Favours Deferred at Ritual Altars in Map reappear 25 to 40% sooner" (previously 15 to 40%).
>   + "of the Foundling" now grants "Revived Monsters from Ritual Altars in Map have 35 to 70% increased chance to be Magic" (previously 25 to 70%).
>   + "of the Cult" now grants "Revived Monsters from Ritual Altars in Map have 25 to 40% increased chance to be Rare" (previously 15 to 40%).
>   + "of Omens" now grants "Ritual Favours in Map have 35 to 70% increased chance to be Omens" (previously 25 to 70%).
>   + "of Pathways" now grants "18 to 30% increased Quantity of Waystones dropped by Map Bosses" (previously 10 to 30%).
>   + "of Conquering" now grants "Map Bosses grant 40 to 80% increased Experience" (previously 20 to 80%).
>   + "of Treasure" now grants "35 to 60% increased Rarity of Items dropped by Map Bosses" (previously 20 to 60%).
>   + "of Hoards" now grants "13 to 20% increased Quantity of Items dropped by Map Bosses" (previously 10 to 20%).
>   + "of the Horde" now grants "Abysses in Map spawn 20 to 30% increased Monsters" (previously 15 to 30%).
> * The "of Fleeting" map modifier can now only roll on Tier 11+ Waystones and has a value of 10-15% (previously 21-25%).
> * The [Xesht's Madness](/wiki/Xesht%27s_Madness "Xesht's Madness") Breach Atlas Notable no longer provides "Rare Breach Monsters in your Maps have the Soul Eater Modifier", instead provides Rare Breach Monsters have Onslaught and Rare Breach Monsters have 50% increased Effectiveness.
> * The [Prayer for Wealth](/wiki/Prayer_for_Wealth "Prayer for Wealth") Atlas Passive has been removed, due to Greed Shrines no longer being available.
> * [The High Road](/wiki/The_High_Road "The High Road") no longer provides "Waystones found have 20% chance to be a tier higher", now provides "10% chance for Waystones found in your Maps to be Rare and Corrupted".
> * The [Get out of my head!](/wiki/Get_out_of_my_head%21 "Get out of my head!") and [The mirrors... the mirrors!](/wiki/The_mirrors..._the_mirrors%21 "The mirrors... the mirrors!") Delirium Atlas Notables have swapped places.
> * The Get out of my head! Delirium Atlas Notable has been reworked, it now provides Magic Monsters in your Maps have +25% chance to have an additional Delirium Modifier and 100% increased Rarity of Items dropped by Magic Monsters in Maps with multiple Delirium Modifiers.
> * The [Isn't it tempting?](/wiki/Isn%27t_it_tempting%3F "Isn't it tempting?") Delirium Atlas Notable has been reworked, it now provides Currency which drops from Delirium Monsters in your Maps is stolen by the Map Boss, Each stolen Currency has a +20% chance to be Duplicated upon defeating the Map Boss if under the affects of Delirium.
> * The [It's not real, it's not real!](/wiki/It%27s_not_real%2C_it%27s_not_real%21 "It's not real, it's not real!") Delirium Atlas Notable has been reworked, it now provides Rare Monsters always Manifest Delirium Demons in your Maps, 10% increased Quantity of Items dropped by Rare Monsters with Manifested Delirium Demons in your Maps and Rare Monsters with Manifested Delirium Demons in your Maps grant 30% increased Experience.
> * Waystones can no longer be instilled using [Liquid Emotions](/wiki/Liquid_Emotion "Liquid Emotion").
> * Improved the visuals of [Delirium](/wiki/Delirium "Delirium") fog and added a radius around the player that improves clarity further, this radius has less of a desaturation effect and makes the fog thinner.
> * Delirium no longer has the reward bar indicator, instead Delirium monsters have a chance to drop Liquid Emotions.
> * Delirium Bosses have a guaranteed Liquid Emotion drop and an increased chance to drop higher tier Liquid Emotions.
> * Boss Waves in the [Simulacrum](/wiki/Simulacrum "Simulacrum") also drop a guaranteed Liquid Emotion with a chance of being a higher tier Liquid Emotion.
> * ![](/images/thumb/2/28/Idol_of_Estazunti_inventory_icon.png/16px-Idol_of_Estazunti_inventory_icon.png)[Idols of Estazunti](/wiki/Idol_of_Estazunti "Idol of Estazunti")Idol of EstazuntiStack Size: *10*Grants access to a Sealed Vault on the Atlas"The perfect harmony of architecture and thaumaturgy.
>   My vaults were impenetrable....until it was
>   decided that they wanted to be able to leave."
>   --Estazunti, Architect of the VaultPlace in the Map Device alongside a Waystone to access a Sealed Vault.![](/images/thumb/2/28/Idol_of_Estazunti_inventory_icon.png/78px-Idol_of_Estazunti_inventory_icon.png) are no longer required to unlock [Vaal Vault](/wiki/Vaal_Vault "Vaal Vault") maps. Existing items will be deleted.
> * The [Vaults of Kamasa](/wiki/Vaults_of_Kamasa "Vaults of Kamasa") Unique Map chests are no longer affected by party bonuses.
> * Removed camera zoom out on completion of [tower](/wiki/Tower "Tower") maps.
> * Added an objective icon for activating all checkpoints. When a player activates all checkpoints and completes the map, all map content minimap icons will be revealed.
> * Removed [Breach](/wiki/Breach "Breach"), [Ritual](/wiki/Ritual "Ritual"), [Delirium](/wiki/Delirium "Delirium"), and [Expedition](/wiki/Expedition "Expedition") from the Map Legend as they no longer have icons shown on your Atlas (and instead can be found randomly in maps or added through the use of Precursor Tablets).
>
> ### Monster Changes
>
> [Bosses](/wiki/Boss "Boss") now have an Anti-Burst damage mechanic: Once a boss has finished it's emerge or becomes aggro the damage reduction period starts counting down. The damage reduction tapers down from full effect to no effect over the course of this duration. For every unit the boss moves from it's starting location the damage reduction will fall off even faster. Bosses which cannot or barely move have a shorter damage reduction period.
>
> * Improved the visibility of the explosive fungus encountered in [The Grim Tangle](/wiki/The_Grim_Tangle "The Grim Tangle")
> * Improved the visibility of the explosive fungus spawned by the [Fungal Proliferator](/wiki/Fungal_Proliferator "Fungal Proliferator") monster type
> * Improved the mid fight phase change sequence of the [final Act 2 boss](/wiki/Jamanra%2C_the_Abomination "Jamanra, the Abomination")
> * Improved the first phase change sequence of the [final Act 4 boss](/wiki/Tavakai%2C_the_Chieftain "Tavakai, the Chieftain")
> * Improved the behaviour of the [Great White One](/wiki/Great_White_One "Great White One") boss.
> * Made various improvements to [Rogue Exile](/wiki/Rogue_Exile "Rogue Exile") behaviour.
> * Re-enabled the following Rogue Exiles; Taua, the Ruthless, Ulfred, the Afflicted, Drusian, the Artillerist and Doran, the Deft.
> * [The Blind Beast](/wiki/The_Blind_Beast "The Blind Beast") in [Isle of Kin](/wiki/Isle_of_Kin "Isle of Kin") now drops a Blank Greater Rune. This can be exchanged with [Dannig](/wiki/Dannig "Dannig") in [Kingsmarch](/wiki/Kingsmarch "Kingsmarch") for a Greater Rune of your choosing (from a selection).
> * The Blind Beast no longer drops a Bile-soaked Tome. Instead, the [Dark Mists](/wiki/Dark_Mists "Dark Mists") quest now grants a ![](/images/thumb/8/80/Book_of_Specialisation_inventory_icon.png/16px-Book_of_Specialisation_inventory_icon.png)[Mist-shrouded Tome](/wiki/Mist-shrouded_Tome "Mist-shrouded Tome")Mist-shrouded TomeGrants two [Weapon Set Passive Skill Points](/wiki/Weapon_Set_Passive_Skill_Points "Weapon Set Passive Skill Points")A Book of Specialisation. Right-click to gain two [Weapon Set Passive Skill Points](/wiki/Weapon_Set_Passive_Skill_Points "Weapon Set Passive Skill Points").![](/images/thumb/8/80/Book_of_Specialisation_inventory_icon.png/156px-Book_of_Specialisation_inventory_icon.png) (which grants two Weapon Set Passive Skill Points) in addition to its existing rewards (Uncut Skill Gem and Gold).
> * You can now open a Town Portal in [Olroth](/wiki/Olroth "Olroth")'s arena after he has been defeated.
> * [Kosis](/wiki/Kosis/edit?redlink=1 "Kosis (page does not exist)")'s Lighting Barrage skill should no longer hit with 9 projectiles at point blank range.
> * Adjusted the following monsters (and subsequently their spectre variant):
> * [Frost Wraith](/wiki/Frost_Wraith "Frost Wraith"): Lowered Spectre Cost, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Lightning Wraith](/wiki/Lightning_Wraith "Lightning Wraith"): Lowered Spectre Cost.
> * [Vile Vulture](/wiki/Vile_Vulture "Vile Vulture"): Improved Monster AI, Lowered Spectre Cost.
> * [Faridun Impaler](/wiki/Faridun_Impaler "Faridun Impaler"): Improved Monster AI, Lowered Spectre Cost.
> * [Bramble Hulk](/wiki/Bramble_Hulk "Bramble Hulk"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Skeletal Reaper](/wiki/Skeletal_Reaper/edit?redlink=1 "Skeletal Reaper (page does not exist)"): Improved Monster AI, Rebalanced monster power resulting in a lower Spectre Cost.
> * [Cultist Archer](/wiki/Cultist_Archer "Cultist Archer"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Blackstrider](/wiki/Blackstrider/edit?redlink=1 "Blackstrider (page does not exist)"): Rebalanced monster power resulting in a lower Spectre Cost, Improved Monster AI, Increased the Web Mortar skill damage, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Mud Simulacrum](/wiki/Mud_Simulacrum "Mud Simulacrum"): Slam damage is now more consistant, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Werewolf Prowler](/wiki/Werewolf_Prowler "Werewolf Prowler"): Slightly increased attack damage.
> * [Ancient Ezomyte](/wiki/Ancient_Ezomyte "Ancient Ezomyte"): Adjusted the Lightning Arrow skill to correctly be Attack damage.
> * [Brimstone Crab](/wiki/Brimstone_Crab "Brimstone Crab"): Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Mar Acolyte](/wiki/Mar_Acolyte "Mar Acolyte"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Quadrilla](/wiki/Quadrilla "Quadrilla"): Improved Monster AI.
> * [Iron Sharpshooter](/wiki/Iron_Sharpshooter "Iron Sharpshooter"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Iron Thaumaturgist](/wiki/Iron_Thaumaturgist "Iron Thaumaturgist"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Fungal Proliferator](/wiki/Fungal_Proliferator "Fungal Proliferator"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Vaal Guard's](/wiki/Vaal_Guard "Vaal Guard") which throw Oil and Explosive Grenades now have an 11 second Cooldown on their Oil Grenade (previously 2 seconds).
>
> ### User Interface Changes
>
> * Some interfaces that could not be panelled now allow dual cursors so both players can interact with a UI at the same time.
> * [Support gem](/wiki/Support_gem "Support gem") compatibility of all equipped skills is now shown when hovering a support gem in the gemcutting interface.
> * On the [waypoint](/wiki/Waypoint "Waypoint") world map, selecting underground locations featured on the overworld map will now immediately teleport you to the selected location, instead of toggling to the underground map view.
> * Added a 'quick search' feature to the Stat Filters in the [Trade Market](/wiki/Trade_Market/edit?redlink=1 "Trade Market (page does not exist)").
> * Stackable items will no longer be merged into existing item stacks when ctrl-clicking items into [Merchant's Tabs](/wiki/Merchant%27s_Tab "Merchant's Tab").
> * Optimised item search for the in-game market browser.
> * Your current [Rage](/wiki/Rage "Rage") is no longer displayed in your buff bar. Instead, there is now a Rage meter next to the mana globe.
> * The Cursor Size option has been changed to a slider.
> * Added a new Cursor Tracking input option for keyboard and mouse users, which allows skills to continue updating their target location/direction even after the skill's input key is released. This is particularly impactful for skills such as ![](/images/thumb/a/a9/Rolling_Slam_inventory_icon.png/16px-Rolling_Slam_inventory_icon.png)[Rolling Slam](/wiki/Rolling_Slam "Rolling Slam")Rolling Slam[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Slam](/wiki/Slam_%28gem_tag%29 "Slam (gem tag)")
>   Tier: *1*
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(14-96) Mana*Requires: *[One Hand Mace](/wiki/Mace "Mace"), [Two Hand Mace](/wiki/Mace "Mace")*[Slam](/wiki/Slam "Slam") the ground to [Stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") enemies and [knock them away](/wiki/Knockback "Knockback"), then continue forward and perform a devastating second [Slam](/wiki/Slam "Slam").Rolling Slam
>   +1.5 seconds to Total [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Time
>   While [Dual Wielding](/wiki/Dual_Wielding "Dual Wielding"), both weapons hit with 30% less damage
>
>   First Slam
>   Attack Damage: (90–367)% of base
>   50% more Stun buildup
>   Impact radius is 1.4 metres
>
>   Second Slam
>   Attack Damage: (180–735)% of base
>   50% more Damage against Heavy Stunned Enemies
>   Impact radius is 1.8 metres
>
>    *Additional Effects From 1-20% Quality:
>    *(5-100)% increased [Stun Threshold](/wiki/Stun_Threshold "Stun Threshold") while using Skill**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/b/b0/Rolling_Slam_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3ARolling_Slam_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/a/a9/Rolling_Slam_inventory_icon.png/78px-Rolling_Slam_inventory_icon.png) and ![](/images/thumb/c/c4/Whirling_Assault_inventory_icon.png/16px-Whirling_Assault_inventory_icon.png)[Whirling Assault](/wiki/Whirling_Assault "Whirling Assault")Whirling Assault[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Strike](/wiki/Strike_%28gem_tag%29 "Strike (gem tag)")
>   Tier: *11*
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(18-126) Mana*
>   Attack Speed: *85% of base*
>   Attack Damage: *(40-163)% of base*Requires: *[Quarterstaff](/wiki/Quarterstaff "Quarterstaff")*Advance while hitting enemies around you with a series of spinning [Strikes](/wiki/Strike "Strike").+1 second to Total [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Time
>   +14 to [Melee](/wiki/Melee "Melee") [Strike](/wiki/Strike "Strike") Range
>   (1-20)% more Area of Effect
>
>    *Additional Effects From 1-20% Quality:
>    *(0.75-15)% more [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Speed**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/1/1f/Whirling_Assault_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AWhirling_Assault_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/c/c4/Whirling_Assault_inventory_icon.png/78px-Whirling_Assault_inventory_icon.png), but affects a wide variety of skills. By default this option is enabled in WASD mode and disabled in click to move mode.
> * When switching between controller and keyboard in the character selection screen, the game will remember if you used WASD or not.
> * **Refactored Couch Coop player interfaces:**
>   + Some interfaces that could not be panelled now allow dual cursors so both players can interact with a UI at the same time.
>   + Most player interfaces will now be panelled to minimise disruptions and to improve the gameplay flow in towns. Both players can have different panelled interfaces open at the same time.
>
> ### Microtransaction Changes
>
> * The [Wardrobe](/wiki/Wardrobe_Decoration/edit?redlink=1 "Wardrobe Decoration (page does not exist)") hideout decoration now visually indicates, and opens to your Wishlist page, when a [Microtransaction](/wiki/Microtransaction "Microtransaction") you've previously wishlisted is on sale.
> * Enabled the following existing Rare Finisher Effect microtransactions for use in Path of Exile 2: [Aesir Lightning Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Aesir_Lightning_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Aesir Lightning Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Anchor Drop Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Anchor_Drop_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Anchor Drop Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Black Hole Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Black_Hole_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Black Hole Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Blackstar Meteor Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Blackstar_Meteor_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Blackstar Meteor Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Consuming Tentacle Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Consuming_Tentacle_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Consuming Tentacle Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Dragon Fire Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Dragon_Fire_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Dragon Fire Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Necrotic Flames Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Necrotic_Flames_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Necrotic Flames Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Shark Attack Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Shark_Attack_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Shark Attack Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)"), [Sulphite Shatter Rare Finisher Effect](/wiki/Sulphite_Shatter_Rare_Finisher_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Sulphite Shatter Rare Finisher Effect (page does not exist)").
> * Enabled the existing [Cathedral Armour](/wiki/Cathedral_Armour/edit?redlink=1 "Cathedral Armour (page does not exist)") Set, [Dreadspire Armour](/wiki/Dreadspire_Armour/edit?redlink=1 "Dreadspire Armour (page does not exist)") Set, [Corsair Armour](/wiki/Corsair_Armour/edit?redlink=1 "Corsair Armour (page does not exist)") Set, [Corsair Hood](/wiki/Corsair_Hood/edit?redlink=1 "Corsair Hood (page does not exist)"), [Corsair Helmet](/wiki/Corsair_Helmet/edit?redlink=1 "Corsair Helmet (page does not exist)"), [Abyss Core Armour](/wiki/Abyss_Core_Armour/edit?redlink=1 "Abyss Core Armour (page does not exist)") Set, [Abyss Core Crown](/wiki/Abyss_Core_Crown/edit?redlink=1 "Abyss Core Crown (page does not exist)"), [Siren Armour Set](/wiki/Siren_Armour_Set/edit?redlink=1 "Siren Armour Set (page does not exist)"), [Siren Hood](/wiki/Siren_Hood/edit?redlink=1 "Siren Hood (page does not exist)"), [Harmonious Armour Set](/wiki/Harmonious_Armour_Set/edit?redlink=1 "Harmonious Armour Set (page does not exist)"), [Gargoyle Armour](/wiki/Gargoyle_Armour/edit?redlink=1 "Gargoyle Armour (page does not exist)") Set and [Glimmerwood Hat](/wiki/Glimmerwood_Hat/edit?redlink=1 "Glimmerwood Hat (page does not exist)") microtransactions for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Astral](/wiki/Astral_Oblivion_Weapon_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Astral Oblivion Weapon Effect (page does not exist)") and [Onyx Oblivion Weapon Effect](/wiki/Onyx_Oblivion_Weapon_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Onyx Oblivion Weapon Effect (page does not exist)") microtransactions for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Stygian](/wiki/Stygian_Character_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Stygian Character Effect (page does not exist)") and [Ebony Character Effect](/wiki/Ebony_Character_Effect/edit?redlink=1 "Ebony Character Effect (page does not exist)") microtransactions for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Hummingbird Pet](/wiki/Hummingbird_Pet/edit?redlink=1 "Hummingbird Pet (page does not exist)") microtransaction for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Gorgon Shield](/wiki/Gorgon_Shield/edit?redlink=1 "Gorgon Shield (page does not exist)") microtransaction for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Celestial Wings](/wiki/Celestial_Wings/edit?redlink=1 "Celestial Wings (page does not exist)") and [Jaeger Cloak](/wiki/Jaeger_Cloak/edit?redlink=1 "Jaeger Cloak (page does not exist)") microtransactions for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Lightning Footprints](/wiki/Lightning_Footprints/edit?redlink=1 "Lightning Footprints (page does not exist)") microtransaction for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Enabled the existing [Celestial Tree Hideout Decoration](/wiki/Celestial_Tree_Hideout_Decoration/edit?redlink=1 "Celestial Tree Hideout Decoration (page does not exist)") microtransaction for use in Path of Exile 2.
> * Added a [stash tab](/wiki/Stash_tab "Stash tab") [affinity](/wiki/Affinity "Affinity") for [Abyss](/wiki/Abyss "Abyss") items.
>
> ### Bug Fixes
>
> * Fixed a bug where effects that spread an [Ignite](/wiki/Ignite "Ignite") were incorrectly just inflicting a single hit's worth of [Flammability](/wiki/Flammability "Flammability") when it tried to spread, and only Igniting if flammability was high enough at that time.
> * Fixed an issue where ![](/images/thumb/d/da/Lightning_Warp_inventory_icon.png/16px-Lightning_Warp_inventory_icon.png)[Lightning Warp](/wiki/Lightning_Warp "Lightning Warp")Lightning Warp[Spell](/wiki/Spell_%28gem_tag%29 "Spell (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning_%28gem_tag%29 "Lightning (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Remnant](/wiki/Remnant_%28gem_tag%29 "Remnant (gem tag)")

>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(8-83) Mana*
>   Cast Time: *0.50 sec*

Can also be used on Ball Lightning [Projectiles](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile"). On teleport, the target is destroyed, and the explosion deals [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") damage to surrounding enemies. If targeting an enemy, the explosion also creates [Shocked Ground](/wiki/Shocked_Ground "Shocked Ground"). Creates a [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") [Infusion](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion") on successful use. Highlights enemies that can be [Culled](/wiki/Cull "Cull").Deals (2-54) to (30-1032) [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") Damage
>   Explosion and [Shocked Ground](/wiki/Shocked_Ground "Shocked Ground") radius are 3 metres

>   [Debuff](/wiki/Debuff "Debuff") duration is 4 seconds
