> * Fixed several bugs allowing stats affecting charge gain to effectively double dip. Chances to gain additional charges now only rolls before effects that change the type of change gained (such as Resonance keystone) - previously could roll twice, once before and once after. Similarly, both the above effects are only checked before effects that cause other things to gain your charges for you (such as Conduit keystone). This means only the original charge generator's stats affect the type and number of charges they give out in this way.
> * Fixed a bug where ![](/images/thumb/e/ec/Vaulting_Impact_inventory_icon.png/16px-Vaulting_Impact_inventory_icon.png)[Vaulting Impact](/wiki/Vaulting_Impact "Vaulting Impact")Vaulting Impact[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Slam](/wiki/Slam_%28gem_tag%29 "Slam (gem tag)"), [Physical](/wiki/Physical_%28gem_tag%29 "Physical (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Travel](/wiki/Travel_%28gem_tag%29 "Travel (gem tag)"), [Payoff](/wiki/Payoff_%28gem_tag%29 "Payoff (gem tag)")

> ### Updates for 8-12-2025
>
> #### New Patch Notes
>
> ##### Player Changes
>
> * When [Parrying](/wiki/Parry "Parry"), you now hit all enemies in an area in front of you, in addition to the enemy who instigated the Parry.
> * ![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Item_inventory_icon.png/16px-Item_inventory_icon.png)[Parry](/wiki/Parry "Parry")Parry[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Physical](/wiki/Physical_%28gem_tag%29 "Physical (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Channelling](/wiki/Channelling_%28gem_tag%29 "Channelling (gem tag)")
>   Level: *1*
>   Attack Time: *0.75 sec*
>   Critical Strike Chance: *5.00%*
>   Attack Damage: *65% of base*Requires: *[Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler")*Ready your [Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler") to parry the next [Strike](/wiki/Strike "Strike") or [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") that would [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") you, [Blocking](/wiki/Block "Block") the [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") and retaliating with a quick sweep that leaves enemies off balance, causing them to take massively increased [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") damage for a short duration. Parrying causes you to accumulate [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup. You cannot [Evade](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") a [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") you could parry, but [Evasion](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") instead grants an equal chance to avoid this [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup.Can't be [Evaded](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion")
>   400% more [Stun](/wiki/Stun "Stun") buildup
>   Can [Block](/wiki/Block "Block") [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") from enemies within 1 metre
>   Can [Block](/wiki/Block "Block") [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") from enemies within 1.5 metres
>   [Parried Debuff](/wiki/Parried_Debuff "Parried Debuff") makes targets take 50% more [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Damage
>   [Parried](/wiki/Parried "Parried") [Debuff](/wiki/Debuff "Debuff") duration is 2 seconds
>   3 to 4 Added [Physical](/wiki/Physical "Physical") Damage per 5 [Evasion Rating](/wiki/Evasion_Rating "Evasion Rating") on [Buckler](/wiki/Buckler "Buckler")Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/c/c7/Parry_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AParry_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Item_inventory_icon.png/78px-Item_inventory_icon.png) now always hits the enemy you parried, regardless of distance.
> * [Sprinting](/wiki/Sprint "Sprint") no longer prevents [heavy stun](/wiki/Heavy_stun "Heavy stun") buildup decay.
>

>   Category: *Ambrosia*
>   Tier: *3*Support Requirements: *+5 Int*Supports Skills you use yourself which damage enemies with [Hits](/wiki/Hit "Hit"). Supported Skills consume a percentage of your maximum Mana [Flask](/wiki/Flask "Flask") charges, [Gaining](/wiki/Damage_Gained_as_extra_X "Damage Gained as extra X") a percentage of damage as extra [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") damage per Mana [Flask](/wiki/Flask "Flask") charge consumed.Supported Skills consume 35% of your maximum Mana [Flask](/wiki/Flask "Flask") charges on use
>   Supported Skills [Gain](/wiki/Gain "Gain") 1% of Damage as extra [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") Damage per Mana [Flask](/wiki/Flask "Flask") charge consumedPlace into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. You cannot have multiple Support Gems of the same Category socketed within one Skill.![](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ambrosia_I_inventory_icon.png/78px-Ambrosia_I_inventory_icon.png) as a Tier-III support, which consumes 35% of your Mana Flask's maximum charges, granting 1% of damage as extra Lightning damage per charge consumed.
> * Ambrosia support is now Ambrosia I and consumes 14% of your Mana Flask's maximum charges, granting 2% of damage as extra Lightning damage per charge consumed (previously consumed 20% and granted 3% per charge consumed).
> * ![](/images/thumb/2/2e/Magnified_Area_I_inventory_icon.png/16px-Magnified_Area_I_inventory_icon.png)[Magnified Area II](/wiki/Magnified_Area_II "Magnified Area II")Magnified Area II[Support](/wiki/Support_%28gem_tag%29 "Support (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)")
>   Category: *Increased Area of Effect*
>   Tier: *3*
>   Cost & Reservation Multiplier: *130%*Support Requirements: *+5 Int*Supports any skill with an area of effect, making it larger.Supported Skills have 45% increased Area of EffectPlace into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. You cannot have multiple Support Gems of the same Category socketed within one Skill.![](/images/thumb/2/2e/Magnified_Area_I_inventory_icon.png/78px-Magnified_Area_I_inventory_icon.png) support gem no longer causes the supported Skill to deal less damage.

> ##### Item Changes
>
> * ![](/images/thumb/6/60/Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png/16px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png)[Omen of Homogenising Exaltation](/wiki/Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation "Omen of Homogenising Exaltation")Omen of Homogenising ExaltationStack Size: *10*While this item is active in your inventory your next
>   Exalted Orb will add a Modifier of the same
>   type as an existing Modifier on the ItemRight click this item in your inventory to set it to be active. This item is consumed when triggered.![](/images/thumb/6/60/Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png/78px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Exaltation_inventory_icon.png) and the ![](/images/thumb/0/0b/Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation_inventory_icon.png/16px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation_inventory_icon.png)[Omen of Homogenising Coronation](/wiki/Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation "Omen of Homogenising Coronation")Omen of Homogenising CoronationStack Size: *10*While this item is active in your inventory your next
>   Regal Orb will add a Modifier of the same
>   type as an existing Modifier on the ItemRight click this item in your inventory to set it to be active. This item is consumed when triggered.![](/images/thumb/0/0b/Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation_inventory_icon.png/78px-Omen_of_Homogenising_Coronation_inventory_icon.png) have been disabled from dropping. Existing items are still functional.

> * ![](/images/thumb/0/0b/Hefty_Quarterstaff_inventory_icon.png/4px-Hefty_Quarterstaff_inventory_icon.png)[Hefty Quarterstaff](/wiki/Hefty_Quarterstaff "Hefty Quarterstaff")Hefty QuarterstaffQuartertaff

>   Critical Strike Chance: *10.00%*
>   Attacks per Second: *1.30*

Existing items will not have this implicit.
> * A new endgame quarterstaff has been added with the same implicit as Hefty Quarterstaff.

> ##### Microtransaction Changes
>
> * Added a [stash tab](/wiki/Stash_tab "Stash tab") [affinity](/wiki/Affinity "Affinity") for [Abyss](/wiki/Abyss "Abyss") items.
>
> ##### Bug Fixes
>
> * Fixed a bug where you couldn't pick up items or interact with objects while mounted on a ![](/images/thumb/3/30/Rhoa_Mount_inventory_icon.png/16px-Rhoa_Mount_inventory_icon.png)[Rhoa Mount](/wiki/Rhoa_Mount "Rhoa Mount")Rhoa Mount[Minion](/wiki/Minion_%28gem_tag%29 "Minion (gem tag)"), [Buff](/wiki/Buff_%28gem_tag%29 "Buff (gem tag)"), [Companion](/wiki/Companion_%28gem_tag%29 "Companion (gem tag)"), [Persistent](/wiki/Persistent_%28gem_tag%29 "Persistent (gem tag)")
>   Tier: *14*
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Reservation: *100 Spirit*Harnesses a [Companion](/wiki/Companion "Companion") Rhoa you can mount while you're wielding a [Bow](/wiki/Bow "Bow") or [Spear](/wiki/Spear "Spear"). While mounted you can use [Bow](/wiki/Bow "Bow"), thrown [Spear](/wiki/Spear "Spear"), and [Mark](/wiki/Mark "Mark") Skills, and are much less slowed while using Skills, but being [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit") will cause [Heavy Stun](/wiki/Heavy_Stun "Heavy Stun") buildup. While you aren't mounted, the Rhoa will attack your enemies alongside you with its beak, but can be damaged.100% reduced Movement Speed Penalty from
>   using Skills while mounted
>
>    *Additional Effects From 1-20% Quality:
>    *Minions have (1-20)% more Maximum Life**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/9/96/Rhoa_Mount_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3ARhoa_Mount_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/3/30/Rhoa_Mount_inventory_icon.png/78px-Rhoa_Mount_inventory_icon.png).
> * Fixed an instance in which you would gain the benefits of Rhoa Mount while you are dismounted.
> * Fixed a bug where Ambrosia Support and Concoct Support were granting their full benefits when only a portion of their desired flask charge consumption could be fulfilled. Both supports now only consume flask charges if their desired amount can be fully fulfilled.
>
> #### Updated Patch Notes
>
> * Added a new [Mountain Splitter](/wiki/Mountain_Splitter "Mountain Splitter") Ascendancy Passive Skill which grants Every Third Slam Skill that doesn't create Fissures which you use yourself causes 3 additional Aftershocks ahead and to each side of the initial area. Requires [Crushing Impacts](/wiki/Crushing_Impacts "Crushing Impacts").
> * ![](/images/thumb/9/9f/Queen_of_the_Forest_inventory_icon.png/11px-Queen_of_the_Forest_inventory_icon.png)[Queen of the Forest](/wiki/Queen_of_the_Forest "Queen of the Forest")Queen of the Forest
>   Smuggler CoatEvasion: *(948-1084)*
>   Movement Speed: *-3.0%*Requires Level *51*, *82* Dex(250-300)% increased [Evasion](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") Rating
>   -(15-10)% to [Fire Resistance](/wiki/Fire_Resistance "Fire Resistance")
>   +(25-30)% to [Cold Resistance](/wiki/Cold_Resistance "Cold Resistance")
>   +(10-15)% to [Lightning Resistance](/wiki/Lightning_Resistance "Lightning Resistance")
>   Increases Movement Speed by 25%, plus 1% per 600 [Evasion](/wiki/Evasion "Evasion") Rating, up to [a maximum of 75](/wiki/Maximim/edit?redlink=1 "Maximim (page does not exist)")%
>   Other Modifiers to Movement Speed except for Sprinting do not applyShedding away her regal past,
>   she forged a new destiny.
>   Sacrificing the ephemeral joys of man,
>   she embraced the eternal grasp of nature.
>   Seizing her one true wish,
>   she found peace at last.![](/images/thumb/9/9f/Queen_of_the_Forest_inventory_icon.png/156px-Queen_of_the_Forest_inventory_icon.png) now Increases Movement Speed by 25%, plus 1% per 600 Evasion Rating, up to a maximum of 75%. Other Modifiers to Movement Speed except for Sprinting do not apply (previously did not have the constant 25%, was and uncapped, was per 800, and Sprinting was not an exception) 800) This change does not affect existing items other than to apply the cap and the constant 25% increase, but the per Evasion rating value, which value will not be changed on existing items. This value can be updated using a Divine Orb.

> ### Updates for 9-12-2025
>
> #### New Patch Notes
>
> ##### Player changes
>
> * You now lose 5 [rage](/wiki/Rage "Rage") per second if you have not taken damage or gained rage in the past 4 seconds (from 10 rage per second if not taken damage or gained rage in the past 2 seconds).
>

>   Gain (3-6) [Rage](/wiki/Rage "Rage") on [Hit](/wiki/Hit "Hit")The first Karui born on the fringes of the Vaal empire developed a blood fever born of corruption.![](/images/thumb/e/e0/Hateforge_inventory_icon.png/156px-Hateforge_inventory_icon.png) Unique now has "300-400% increased Armour" (previously 50-80%), existing items can be updated using a Divine Orb. Now has Gain a random charge on reaching maximum Rage, no more than once every 3-6 seconds (previously 1-3 charges). It now also rolls "Gain 3-6 Rage on Hit", this change does not affect existing versions of the item.
>
> ##### Item changes
>
> * ![](/images/thumb/b/b4/Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png/16px-Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png)[Rabbit Idol](/wiki/Rabbit_Idol "Rabbit Idol")Rabbit IdolStack Size: *10*Body Armours: 5% increased [Rarity of Items](/wiki/Rarity "Rarity") found
>   Sceptres: 10% increased [Spirit](/wiki/Spirit "Spirit")Bonded:
>   Body Armours: 5% increased Quantity of Gold Dropped by Slain Enemies
>   Sceptres: [Minions](/wiki/Minion "Minion") have 30% increased [Cooldown Recovery Rate](/wiki/Cooldown_Recovery_Rate "Cooldown Recovery Rate") for [Command](/wiki/Command "Command") SkillsPlace into an empty [Augment](/wiki/Augment "Augment") Socket in a Weapon or Armour to apply its effect to that item. Once socketed it cannot be retrieved but can be replaced by other [Augment](/wiki/Augment "Augment") items.![](/images/thumb/b/b4/Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png/78px-Rabbit_Idol_inventory_icon.png) now grants 5% increased Rarity of Items found (from 8%).

>   [Bow](/wiki/Bow "Bow") or [Crossbow](/wiki/Crossbow "Crossbow"): (8-10)% increased [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") SpeedRight click this item then left click a Magic item to apply it.![](/images/thumb/6/66/Lesser_Essence_of_Haste_inventory_icon.png/78px-Lesser_Essence_of_Haste_inventory_icon.png) now adds (8-10)% increased Attack Speed to Bows and Crossbows, this is unchanged on Melee Weapons. (Now only Wands and Staves).
>
> ##### Endgame changes
>
> * [The Arbiter of Ash](/wiki/The_Arbiter_of_Ash "The Arbiter of Ash") will now phase transition at a lower life threshold and will heal to full during the transition.
>
> ##### Monster changes
>
> * Adjusted the following monsters (and subsequently their spectre variant):
> * [Frost Wraith](/wiki/Frost_Wraith "Frost Wraith"): Lowered Spectre Cost, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Lightning Wraith](/wiki/Lightning_Wraith "Lightning Wraith"): Lowered Spectre Cost.
> * [Vile Vulture](/wiki/Vile_Vulture "Vile Vulture"): Improved Monster AI, Lowered Spectre Cost.
> * [Faridun Impaler](/wiki/Faridun_Impaler "Faridun Impaler"): Improved Monster AI, Lowered Spectre Cost.
> * [Bramble Hulk](/wiki/Bramble_Hulk "Bramble Hulk"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Skeletal Reaper](/wiki/Skeletal_Reaper/edit?redlink=1 "Skeletal Reaper (page does not exist)"): Improved Monster AI, Rebalanced monster power resulting in a lower Spectre Cost.
> * [Cultist Archer](/wiki/Cultist_Archer "Cultist Archer"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Blackstrider](/wiki/Blackstrider/edit?redlink=1 "Blackstrider (page does not exist)"): Rebalanced monster power resulting in a lower Spectre Cost, Improved Monster AI, Increased the Web Mortar skill damage, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Mud Simulacrum](/wiki/Mud_Simulacrum "Mud Simulacrum"): Slam damage is now more consistant, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Werewolf Prowler](/wiki/Werewolf_Prowler "Werewolf Prowler"): Slightly increased attack damage.
> * [Ancient Ezomyte](/wiki/Ancient_Ezomyte "Ancient Ezomyte"): Adjusted the Lightning Arrow skill to correctly be Attack damage.
> * [Brimstone Crab](/wiki/Brimstone_Crab "Brimstone Crab"): Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Mar Acolyte](/wiki/Mar_Acolyte "Mar Acolyte"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Quadrilla](/wiki/Quadrilla "Quadrilla"): Improved Monster AI.
> * [Iron Sharpshooter](/wiki/Iron_Sharpshooter "Iron Sharpshooter"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Iron Thaumaturgist](/wiki/Iron_Thaumaturgist "Iron Thaumaturgist"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Fungal Proliferator](/wiki/Fungal_Proliferator "Fungal Proliferator"): Improved Monster AI, Reduced Cooldown of some skills.
> * [Vaal Guard's](/wiki/Vaal_Guard "Vaal Guard") which throw Oil and Explosive Grenades now have an 11 second Cooldown on their Oil Grenade (previously 2 seconds).
>

Now has 100% reduced Movement Speed penalty from using Skills while mounted (previously 80%). Now reserves 100 spirit (previously 60).

> ### Updates for 11-12-2025
>
> #### New Patch Notes
>
> ##### Player Changes
>
> * [Totem](/wiki/Totem "Totem") Placement speed now also scales the speed at which Totems emerge.
>
> ##### Passive Tree Changes
>
> * [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Area passive skills on the Passive Tree have been halved, now granting 10% Curse Area of Effect (previously 20%). The Zone of Control Notable skill now grants 20% increased Curse Area of Effect (previously 40%) but also grants 10% increased Curse Magnitudes (previously 8%). The Curse Area small passives on the [Lich](/wiki/Lich "Lich") and [Abyssal Lich](/wiki/Abyssal_Lich "Abyssal Lich") now grant 15% increased Curse Area (previously 25%).
>
> ##### Support Changes
>
> * Added the missing Chaos tag to ![](/images/thumb/f/f2/Extraction_inventory_icon.png/16px-Extraction_inventory_icon.png)[extraction](/wiki/Extraction "Extraction")Extraction[Support](/wiki/Support_%28gem_tag%29 "Support (gem tag)"), [Spell](/wiki/Spell_%28gem_tag%29 "Spell (gem tag)"), [Chaos](/wiki/Chaos_%28gem_tag%29 "Chaos (gem tag)")
>   Category: *Extraction*
>   Tier: *3*Support Requirements: *+5 Int*Supports [Spell](/wiki/Spell "Spell") Skills which cause [Damaging Hits](/wiki/Damaging_Hit "Damaging Hit"). Using supported [Spells](/wiki/Spell "Spell") will cause you to [Sacrifice](/wiki/Sacrifice_%28keyword%29 "Sacrifice (keyword)") a portion of your Life on use, gaining extra [Chaos](/wiki/Chaos "Chaos") Damage in exchange. Does not support [Persistent](/wiki/Persistent "Persistent") Skills, [Minion](/wiki/Minion "Minion") Skills, or [Triggered](/wiki/Trigger "Trigger") Skills.Supported Skills [Gain](/wiki/Gain "Gain") 35% of Damage as extra [Chaos](/wiki/Chaos "Chaos") Damage

>   Category: *Second Wind*
>   Tier: *5*

Can no longer support Meta skills.

>    *Additional Effects From 1-20% Quality:
>    *(0.5-10)% increased [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") [Magnitudes](/wiki/Magnitude "Magnitude")**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/9/9e/Despair_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3ADespair_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/4/48/Despair_inventory_icon.png/78px-Despair_inventory_icon.png) and ![](/images/thumb/3/38/Ascendancy_inventory_icon.png/16px-Ascendancy_inventory_icon.png)[Inevitable Agony](/wiki/Inevitable_Agony "Inevitable Agony")Inevitable Agony[Spell](/wiki/Spell_%28gem_tag%29 "Spell (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Curse](/wiki/Curse_%28gem_tag%29 "Curse (gem tag)")
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(41-178) Mana*
>   Cast Time: *0.70 sec*[Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") all targets in an area after a short delay, causing a portion of Damage they take from [Hits](/wiki/Hit "Hit") to be tracked by the [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") debuff. When the debuff's duration expires, they take that tracked damage again, all at once.Ignores [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") limit
>   [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") applies after 1.5 seconds delay
>   [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") radius is (1.5-3.1) metres
>   [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") duration is (6-7.4) seconds
>   [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") targets take 50% of [Hit Damage](/wiki/Hit_Damage "Hit Damage") dealt to them while [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") again when [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") expires
>   Taking [Damage](/wiki/Hit "Hit") again this way cannot inflict Ailments on the [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") target
>
>    *Additional Effects From 1-20% Quality:
>    *[Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") zone erupts after (0.5-10)% reduced delay**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/6/64/Inevitable_Agony_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AInevitable_Agony_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/3/38/Ascendancy_inventory_icon.png/78px-Ascendancy_inventory_icon.png) now have lowered radius scaling for Gem Level 20+, increasing by 0.1 metres every 3 levels (previously every level).
> * These changes are accompanied by a rework to ![](/images/thumb/0/0c/Doedre%27s_Undoing_inventory_icon.png/16px-Doedre%27s_Undoing_inventory_icon.png)[Doedre's Undoing](/wiki/Doedre%27s_Undoing "Doedre's Undoing")Doedre's Undoing[Support](/wiki/Support_%28gem_tag%29 "Support (gem tag)"), [Lineage](/wiki/Lineage_%28gem_tag%29 "Lineage (gem tag)"), [Spell](/wiki/Spell_%28gem_tag%29 "Spell (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Trigger](/wiki/Trigger_%28gem_tag%29 "Trigger (gem tag)"), [Chaos](/wiki/Chaos_%28gem_tag%29 "Chaos (gem tag)"), [Curse](/wiki/Curse_%28gem_tag%29 "Curse (gem tag)"), [Hazard](/wiki/Hazard_%28gem_tag%29 "Hazard (gem tag)")
>   Category: *Cursed Ground*Requires Level *65*
>   Support Requirements: *+5 Int*Supports [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Skills. Supported [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Skills create [Hazardous](/wiki/Hazard "Hazard") areas which explode when Enemies enter them, [Cursing](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Enemies and dealing [Chaos](/wiki/Chaos "Chaos") Damage.Support
>   Supported Skills create [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground
>   Enemies on the [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground from a Supported Skill are [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") while within it
>   [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground created by Supported Skills counts as a [Hazard](/wiki/Hazard "Hazard")
>   Maximum 2 areas of [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground
>   [Cursed](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Ground created by Supported Skills triggers Doedre's Dark Design when Enemies enter
>
>   Doedre's Dark Design
>   Explodes and deals Chaos Damage when an Enemy enters the area, applying the supported Curse on Hit.>
>   Deals 7 to 13 Chaos Damage
>   Explosion applies Supported Curse for 3 seconds on Hit
>
> Explosion radius is equal to that of the Cursed Ground
> "Let the meat show us the way. Hail the meat, praise the
> meat. The meat is both debasement and divinity alike. The
> meat shall lead us down the path to true enlightenment."Place into a Skill's Support Gem socket in the Skills Panel to apply its effects to that Skill. You cannot have multiple Support Gems of the same Category socketed within one Skill.![](/images/thumb/0/0c/Doedre%27s_Undoing_inventory_icon.png/78px-Doedre%27s_Undoing_inventory_icon.png) by changing it from scaling off Intellgence to instead scale based on the Supported Curses Level. This opens up the build without having to be Intelligence stacking.

> * ![](/images/thumb/3/35/Firestorm_inventory_icon.png/16px-Firestorm_inventory_icon.png)[Firestorm](/wiki/Firestorm "Firestorm")Firestorm[Spell](/wiki/Spell_%28gem_tag%29 "Spell (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Sustained](/wiki/Sustained_%28gem_tag%29 "Sustained (gem tag)"), [Fire](/wiki/Fire_%28gem_tag%29 "Fire (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Storm](/wiki/Storm_%28gem_tag%29 "Storm (gem tag)")

>   Storm duration is 6 seconds
>   One impact every 0.20 seconds

>    *+(0.01-0.2) metres to impact radius**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/2/2a/Firestorm_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AFirestorm_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/3/35/Firestorm_inventory_icon.png/78px-Firestorm_inventory_icon.png): Now deals 31 to 47 Fire Damage at Gem level 11 (previously 16 to 23), scaling to 111 to 167 Fire Damage at Gem level 20 (previously 56 to 83). Storm radius is now 3 metres (previously 2.8. Now additionally has Fire Infusion grants 100% increased Damage. Fire Infusion now grants +1.5 metres to storm radius (previously 1.8). Fire Infusion now grants 100% increased bolt frequency (previously 200%). Cold infused Ice Bolts now deal 27 to 40 Cold Damage at Gem level 11 (previously 16 to 24), scaling to 95 to 143 Cold Damage at Gem level 20 (previously 58 to 86). Lightning Infused Lightning Bolts now deal 4 to 83 Lightning Damage at Gem level 11 (previously 2 to 44), scaling to 16 to 302 Lightning Damage at Gem level 20 (previously 8 to 156).

> ##### Item Changes
>
> * [Curse](/wiki/Curse "Curse") Area of Effect Mods on [Jewels](/wiki/Jewel "Jewel") have been reduced. Regular Jewels now grant 8-12% Curse Area of Effect (previously 15-25%) and Timeless Jewels now grant 3-6% (previously 6-12%).

>   Cast Time: *1.40 sec*

Can [Consume](/wiki/Consume "Consume") all three types of [Elemental Infusion](/wiki/Elemental_Infusion "Elemental Infusion"), creating a much larger storm when [Fire-Infused](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion"), causing lightning bolts when [Lightning-Infused](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion"), and raining ice bolts when [Cold-Infused](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion").Deals (3-111) to (5-167) [Fire](/wiki/Fire "Fire") Damage
>   Impact radius is 1 metre
>   Storm radius is 3 metres
>   Storm duration is 6 seconds
>   One impact every 0.20 seconds
>   [Fire Infusion](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion") grants 100% increased bolt frequency
>   [Fire Infusion](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion") grants 100% increased Damage
>   [Fire Infusion](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion") grants +1.5 metres to storm radius
>   [Limit](/wiki/Limit "Limit") 1 Firestorm
>   Can Hit each enemy only once every 0.15 seconds
>
>    *Additional Effects From 1-20% Quality:
>    *+(0.01-0.2) metres to impact radius**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/2/2a/Firestorm_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AFirestorm_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/3/35/Firestorm_inventory_icon.png/78px-Firestorm_inventory_icon.png).
> * Fixed several bugs allowing stats affecting charge gain to effectively double dip. Chances to gain additional charges now only rolls before effects that change the type of change gained (such as Resonance keystone) - previously could roll twice, once before and once after. Similarly, both the above effects are only checked before effects that cause other things to gain your charges for you (such as Conduit keystone). This means only the original charge generator's stats affect the type and number of charges they give out in this way.
> * Fixed a bug where ![](/images/thumb/e/ec/Vaulting_Impact_inventory_icon.png/16px-Vaulting_Impact_inventory_icon.png)[Vaulting Impact](/wiki/Vaulting_Impact "Vaulting Impact")Vaulting Impact[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Slam](/wiki/Slam_%28gem_tag%29 "Slam (gem tag)"), [Physical](/wiki/Physical_%28gem_tag%29 "Physical (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Travel](/wiki/Travel_%28gem_tag%29 "Travel (gem tag)"), [Payoff](/wiki/Payoff_%28gem_tag%29 "Payoff (gem tag)")
>   Tier: *5*
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(12-83) Mana*
>   Attack Damage: *(160-422)% of base*Requires: *[Quarterstaff](/wiki/Quarterstaff "Quarterstaff")*Leap forward and [Slam](/wiki/Slam "Slam") the ground, sending out a shockwave. The shockwave applies [Broken Stance](/wiki/Broken_Stance "Broken Stance") to [Dazed](/wiki/Daze "Daze") enemies, causing any [Hits](/wiki/Hit "Hit") against those enemies to deal extra damage.+1 second to Total [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Time
>   Cannot inflict [Daze](/wiki/Daze "Daze")
>   Impact radius is 2.4 metresSkills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/6/6e/Vaulting_Impact_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AVaulting_Impact_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/e/ec/Vaulting_Impact_inventory_icon.png/78px-Vaulting_Impact_inventory_icon.png) and ![](/images/thumb/8/82/Thunderous_Leap_inventory_icon.png/16px-Thunderous_Leap_inventory_icon.png)[Thunderous Leap](/wiki/Thunderous_Leap "Thunderous Leap")Thunderous Leap[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Melee](/wiki/Melee_%28gem_tag%29 "Melee (gem tag)"), [Slam](/wiki/Slam_%28gem_tag%29 "Slam (gem tag)"), [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning_%28gem_tag%29 "Lightning (gem tag)"), [Detonator](/wiki/Detonator_%28gem_tag%29 "Detonator (gem tag)"), [Travel](/wiki/Travel_%28gem_tag%29 "Travel (gem tag)")
>   Tier: *9*
>   Level: *(1-20)*
>   Cost: *(11-76) Mana*
>   Attack Damage: *(110-449)% of base*Requires: *[Spear](/wiki/Spear "Spear")*Leap into the air and plunge your [Spear](/wiki/Spear "Spear") into the ground at the target location, emitting a [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning")-charged shockwave.[Converts](/wiki/Damage_conversion "Damage conversion") 70% of [Physical](/wiki/Physical "Physical") damage to [Lightning](/wiki/Lightning "Lightning") damage
>   +1.1 seconds to Total [Attack](/wiki/Attack "Attack") Time
>   100% more chance to [Shock](/wiki/Shock "Shock")

> #### Updated Patch Notes
>
> * ![](/images/thumb/3/33/Ice_Nova_inventory_icon.png/16px-Ice_Nova_inventory_icon.png)[Ice Nova](/wiki/Ice_Nova "Ice Nova")Ice Nova[Spell](/wiki/Spell_%28gem_tag%29 "Spell (gem tag)"), [AoE](/wiki/AoE_%28gem_tag%29 "AoE (gem tag)"), [Cold](/wiki/Cold_%28gem_tag%29 "Cold (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)"), [Nova](/wiki/Nova_%28gem_tag%29 "Nova (gem tag)")

Casting Ice Nova targeting near a Frostbolt [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile "Projectile") will cause it to originate from the Frostbolt instead of you. [Consumes](/wiki/Effect_Consumption "Effect Consumption") a [Cold](/wiki/Cold "Cold") [Infusion](/wiki/Infusion "Infusion") if possible to leave a patch of [Chilled Ground](/wiki/Chilled_Ground "Chilled Ground").Deals (6-131) to (8-196) [Cold](/wiki/Cold "Cold") Damage

Cold-Infused Ice Nova now Deals 15 to 22 Cold Damage at Gem level 1-20 (previously 13-20), scaling to 448 to 672 Cold Damage at Gem level 20 (previously 394 to 591).
> * ![](/images/thumb/f/ff/Raise_Zombie_inventory_icon.png/16px-Raise_Zombie_inventory_icon.png)[Raise Zombie](/wiki/Raise_Zombie "Raise Zombie")Raise Zombie[Minion](/wiki/Minion_%28gem_tag%29 "Minion (gem tag)"), [Physical](/wiki/Physical_%28gem_tag%29 "Physical (gem tag)"), [Duration](/wiki/Duration_%28gem_tag%29 "Duration (gem tag)")

>    *(1-20)% more [Ignite](/wiki/Ignite "Ignite") duration**Skills can be managed in the Skills Panel.[![](/images/2/2c/Incinerate_skill_icon.png)](/wiki/File%3AIncinerate_skill_icon.png)![](/images/thumb/a/ae/Incinerate_inventory_icon.png/78px-Incinerate_inventory_icon.png): Now additionally deals 11.1 Fire Damage per second at Gem level 1, scaling to 57.5 Fire Damage per second at Gem level 20. Ignited Ground duration is now 8 seconds (previously 4). Now has Ignites from a single use of this Skill Compound if not from Ignited Ground. Quality now grants 20% more Ignite duration (previously ignite magnitude). Now gains 7-2 milliseconds of fuel per Mana spent (previously 10-5). Now can store up to 5 seconds of fuel (previously 10 seconds). No longer has multiple maximum stages or deals 30% more damage per stage. No longer has 50% Less Ignite duration. No longer has Inflicts 80% less Flammability Magnitude. Now ignites as though dealing 16 to 24 Fire damage at Gem level 9 (previously 80-120), scaling to 83 to 124 Fire damage at Gem level 20 (previously 414-622). Incinerate Fuel can no longer be gained while using Incinerate. Incinerate ignites every 75ms, this will be described on the skill gem in a future patch shortly after 0.4.0.
> * ![](/images/thumb/0/08/Ice_Shot_inventory_icon.png/16px-Ice_Shot_inventory_icon.png)[Ice Shot](/wiki/Ice_Shot "Ice Shot")Ice Shot[Attack](/wiki/Attack_%28gem_tag%29 "Attack (gem tag)"), [Projectile](/wiki/Projectile_%28gem_tag%29 "Projectile (gem tag)"), [Cold](/wiki/Cold_%28gem_tag%29 "Cold (gem tag)"), [Barrageable](/wiki/Barrageable_%28gem_tag%29 "Barrageable (gem tag)")

Oil Ground now has Once Ignited, Oil Ground adds 150% of this Attack's Fire Damage as unscalable Damage to the Ignite. Oil now Slows enemy movement speed by 40% (previously 20%).

## Hotfixes

The following hotfixes were deployed after the 0.4.0 patch.

### Hotfix 1

These are the patch notes for hotfix 1.[[2]](#cite_note-Hotfix_1-2)

> * Fixed a client crash that could occur in party play with a [Druid](/wiki/Druid "Druid").
> * Fixed an instance crash.

### Hotfix 2

These are the patch notes for hotfix 2.[[3]](#cite_note-Hotfix_2-3)

> * Fixed a client crash in cosmetics panel while using a controller.
> * Fixed a common client crash.
> * Fixed an instance crash.
> * Fixed an instance crash when using Unearth
> * Fixed an issue where the game would not pause properly sometimes.

### Hotfix 3

These are the patch notes for hotfix 3.[[4]](#cite_note-Hotfix_3-4)

> * Fixed a bug where [Cartographer's Chisels](/wiki/Cartographer%27s_Chisel "Cartographer's Chisel") could drop 😳
> * These items will be automatically removed soon.

### Hotfix 4

These are the patch notes for hotfix 4.[[5]](#cite_note-Hotfix_4-5)

> * Fixed another client crash in cosmetics panel while using a controller.
> * Fixed a client crash in the Guild UI.
> * Fixed a client crash.
> * Fixed a bug where wolves from Pounce/Predator's Mark would deal no damage and be invincible after you die and revive
> * Fixed 5 instance crashes.
> * Fixed a client crash on Vulkan renderer.
> * Fixed a bug where Raging Cry Support wasn't delaying Rage decay.
> * Dying outside of boss encounters in the Atziri's Temple now allows you to respawn at the checkpoint instead of the Vaal Ruins.
> * Thrashing Vines will now more consistently target & hit the same enemy repeatedly, improving its Single Target DPS.
> * Any existing [Cartographer's Chisel](/wiki/Cartographer%27s_Chisel "Cartographer's Chisel") and [Engineer's Orb](/wiki/Engineer%27s_Orb/edit?redlink=1 "Engineer's Orb (page does not exist)") will be deleted upon next login.

### Hotfix 5

These are the patch notes for hotfix 5.[[6]](#cite_note-Hotfix_5-6)

> * Reduced the damage of certain Monster burning ground skills as they were dealing incorrect damage, for example the burning ground from Uxmal, the Beast Lord

### Hotfix 6

These are the patch notes for hotfix 6.[[7]](#cite_note-Hotfix_6-7)

> * Boss Damage Reduction will now fall off faster

### Hotfix 7

These are the patch notes for hotfix 7.[[8]](#cite_note-Hotfix_7-8)

> * Lowered the ignite buildup and damage of the burning ground created from the map mod "Flaming"

### Hotfix 8

These are the patch notes for hotfix 8.[[9]](#cite_note-Hotfix_8-9)

> * Fixed the Stash always opening to a tab with Abyss Affinity set.
> * Fixed 3 instance crashes.

### Hotfix 9

These are the patch notes for hotfix 9.[[10]](#cite_note-Hotfix_9-10)

> * Improved texture streaming for users with low available VRAM.
> * Fixed 2 common client crashes.
> * Fixed a client crash that could occur in the Fortress Map.
> * Fixed a client crash that could occur with Ember Fussilade.
> * Fixed a client crash that could occur in party play.
> * Fixed a bug where reward rooms in the Temple were not Destabilising after completion.

### Hotfix 10

These are the patch notes for hotfix 10.[[11]](#cite_note-Hotfix_10-11)

> * Fixed a client crash caused by the chickens in Clearfell Encampment.
> * Fixed a client crash on Vulkan renderer when resizing the window.
